vitrastāḥ tyakta dāra suta striyaḥ bhraṣṭa adhikārāḥ ṛbhavaḥ viceruḥ channa veṣakāḥ yakṣān mahoragān siddhān sādhyān samara durmadān brahmāṇam padmanābham ca rudram vajriṇam eva ca matvā tṛṇāyitān sarvān lokān bhaṇḍaḥ śaśāsaha atha bhaṇḍa asuram hantum trailokyam ca api rakṣitum tṛtīyam udabhūt rūpam mahā yāga analāt mune yat rūpa śālinīm āhuḥ lalitā para devatām pāśa aṅkuśa dhanuḥ vāṇa pariṣkṛta catur bhujām sā devī parama śaktiḥ para brahma svarūpiṇī jaghāna bhaṇḍa daitya indram yuddhe yuddha viśāradā iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne mohinīprādurbhāvamalakāsuravadhaḥ nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ ca upoddhāta khaṇḍaḥ katham bhaṇḍāsuraḥ jātaḥ katham vā tripurāṃbikā purā dākṣāyaṇīm tyaktvā pituḥ yajña vināśanam ātmānam ātmanā paśyan jñāna ānanda rasa ātmakaḥ upāsyamānaḥ munibhiḥ advandva guṇa lakṣaṇaḥ sā api śaṅkaram ā rādhya cira kālam manasvinī yogena svām tanum tyaktvā sutā āsīt hima bhūbhṛtaḥ sa śailaḥ nāradāt śrutvā rudrāṇi iti sva kanyākām tasya śuśrūṣaṇa arthāya sthāpayāmāsa ca antike etasmin antare devāḥ tārakeṇa hi pīḍitāḥ brahmaṇā uktāḥ samāhūya madanam ca idam abruvan sarga ādau bhagavān brahma sṛjamānaḥ akhilāḥ prajāḥ tapaḥ cacāra suciram manaḥ vāc kāya karmabhiḥ carācara yutam ca etat sṛjāmi tvad prasādataḥ evam uktaḥ vidhātrā tu mahāla kṣmīm udaikṣata tadā prādurabhūḥ tvam hi jagat mohana rūpadhṛk tava āyudha artham dattam ca puṣpabāṇa ikṣu kārmukam asau sṛjati bhūtāni kāraṇena sva karmaṇā amogham bala vīryam te na te moghaḥ parākramaḥ sukumārāṇi amoghāni kusuma astrāṇi te sadā bādhate sakalān lokān asmān api viśeṣataḥ tvām vinā asmin mahā kārye na kaścid pravadet api īṣatkāryam idam kṛtvā trāyasva asmān mahā bala jagāma ātma vināśāya yatas himavataḥ taṭam kim api ārādhaya antam tu dhyāna saṃmīlita īkṣaṇam dadarśa īśānam āsīnam kusuma ṣuḥ udāyudhaḥ ārirādhayiṣuḥ ca ā gāt bibhrāṇā rūpam adbhutam sametya śambhum girijām gandha puṣpa upahārakaiḥ śuśrūṣaṇa parām tatra dadarśa atibalaḥ smaraḥ adṛśyaḥ sarva bhūta ānāt na ati dūre asya saṃsthitaḥ vismṛtya sa hi kāryāṇi bāṇa viddhaḥ antike sthitām gaurīm vilokayāmāsa manmatha āviṣṭa cetanaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā kupitaḥ śūlī trailokya dahana kṣamaḥ tārtīyam cakṣuḥ unmīlya dadāha makaradhvajam śivena evam avajñātā duḥkhitā śailakanyakā atha tat bhasma saṃvīkṣya citrakarmā gaṇeśvaraḥ tad bhasmanā tu puruṣam citra ākāram cakāra saḥ tam vicitra tanum rudraḥ dadarśa agre tu pūruṣam tad kṣaṇāt jāta jīvaḥ abhūt mūrtimān iva manmathaḥ tam citrakarmā bāhubhyām samāliṅgya mudā anvitaḥ iti uktvā śatarudrīyam upādiśat ameya dhīḥ nanāma śataśas rudram śatarudriyam ājapan tatas prasannaḥ bhagavān mahādevaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ vareṇa chandayāmāsa varam vavre sa bālakaḥ ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi rājyam asmai dadau punar etat dṛṣṭvā tu caritam dhātā bhaṇḍ iti bhaṇḍ iti yat uvāca tatas nāmnā bhaṇḍaḥ lokeṣu kathyate dattvā astrāṇi ca śastrāṇi tatra eva antaradhāt ca saḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalita upākhyāne bhaṇḍāsuraprādurbhāvaḥ nāma ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ rudra kopa analāt jātaḥ yatas bhaṇḍaḥ mahā balaḥ athā agacchat mahā tejāḥ śukraḥ daitya purohitaḥ samāyātāḥ ca śataśas daiteyāḥ su mahā balāḥ atha āhūya mayam bhaṇḍaḥ daitya vaṃśya ādi śilpinam tat gatvā śoṇitapuram kuruṣva tvam yathāpuram atha abhiṣiktaḥ śukreṇa daiteyaiḥ ca mahā balaiḥ śuśabhe parayā lakṣmyā tejasā ca samanvitaḥ hiraṇyāya tu yat dattam kirīṭam brahmaṇā purā bhṛgusuta utsṛṣṭam bhaṇḍaḥ bāla arka sannibham na rogaḥ na ca duḥkhāni saṃdadhau yad niṣevaṇāt yasya chāyā niṣaṇṇāḥ tu bādhyante na astra koṭibhiḥ dhanuḥ ca vijayam nāma śaṅkham ca ripu ghātinam anyāni api mahārhāṇi bhūṣaṇāni pradattavān tasya siṃhāsanam prādāt akṣayyam sūrya sannibham tatas siṃhāsana āsīnaḥ sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitaḥ babhūva atīva tejasvī ratnam uttejitam yathā babhūvuḥ atha daiteyāḥ tayā aṣṭau tu mahā balāḥ sumohinī kumudinī citrāṅgī suṃdarī tathā catasraḥ vanitāḥ tasya babhūvuḥ priya darśanāḥ tam asevanta kāla jñāḥ devāḥ sarve sa vāsavāḥ syandanāḥ turagāḥ nāgāḥ pādātāḥ ca sahasraśas saṃbabhūvuḥ mahā kāyāḥ mahāntaḥ jita kāśinaḥ babhūvuḥ dānavāḥ sarve bhṛgu putra mata anugāḥ arcayantaḥ mahādevam āsthitāḥ śiva śāsane gṛhe gṛhe ca yajñāḥ ca saṃbabhūvuḥ samantataḥ ṛcaḥ yajūṃṣi sāmāni mīmāṃsā nyāyaka ādayaḥ pravartante sma daityānām bhūyas pratigṛham tadā yathā āśrameṣu mukhyeṣu munīnām ca dvijanmanām tathā yajñeṣu daityānām bubhujuḥ havya bhojinaḥ evam kṛtavataḥ api asya bhaṇḍasya jita kāśinaḥ ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi vyatītāni kṣaṇa ardha vat hīyamāna balam ca indram saṃprekṣya kamalāpatiḥ sasarja sahasā kāñcid māyām loka vimohinīm tām uvāca tatas māyām devadevaḥ janārdanaḥ tvam hi sarvāṇi bhūtāni mohayantī nija ojasā vicarasva yathākāmam tvām na jñāsyati kaścana tvam tu śīghram itas gatvā bhaṇḍam daiteya nāyakam evam labdhvā varam māyā tam praṇamya janārdanam yayāce apsarasaḥ mukhyāḥ sahāya artham tu kāścana tayā saṃprārthitaḥ bhūyas preṣayāmāsa kāścana tābhiḥ viśvāci mukhyābhiḥ sahitā sā mṛga īkṣaṇā tatra sā mṛgaśāvākṣī mūle caṃpaka śākhinaḥ śrutvā tu vīṇā ninadam dadarśa ca vara aṅganām tām dṛṣṭvā cāru sarva aṅgīm vidyut lekhām iva aparām atha asya mantriṇaḥ abhūvan dṛdaye smaratā api tāḥ taiḥ ca saṃprarthitāḥ tāḥ ca pratiśūśruvuḥ añjasā tāḥ labdhvā mohinī mukhyāḥ nirvṛtim paramām yayuḥ vijahuḥ te tathā yajña kriyāḥ ca anyāḥ śubha āvahāḥ avamāna hataḥ ca āsīt teṣām api purohitaḥ muhūrttam iva teṣām tu yayau abda ayutam tadā mohiteṣu atha daityeṣu sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ praṇamya muni śārdūlam jvalantam iva pāvakam kṛta añjali puṭaḥ bhūtvā deveśaḥ vākyam abravīt bhaviṣyat śobhana ākāram tava āgamana kāraṇam tvad vākya amṛtam ākarṇya śravaṇa ānanda nirbharam aśeṣa duḥkhāni uttīrya kṛtārthaḥ syām muni īśvara nāradaḥ uvāca atha saṃmohitaḥ bhaṇḍaḥ daitya indraḥ viṣṇu māyayā tayā vimuktaḥ lokān trīn daheta agniḥ iva aparaḥ vinā ārādhanataḥ devyāḥ parāśakteḥ tu vāsava purā eva udayataḥ śatroḥ ārādhayata bāliśāḥ ārādhitā bhagavatī sā vaḥ śreyaḥ vidhāsyati evam saṃbodhitaḥ tena śakraḥ deva gaṇa īśvaraḥ tam munim pūjayāmāsa sarva devaiḥ samanvitaḥ parā śakteḥ mahā pūjām cakre akhila suraiḥ samam brahma ātmaja upadiṣṭena kurvatām vidhinā parām devyāḥ tu mahatīm pūjām japa dhyāna rata ātmanām daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi daśa ahāni ca saṃyayuḥ mohitān atha tān dṛṣṭvā bhṛguputraḥ mahāmatiḥ bhaṇḍāsuram samabhyetya nijagāda purohitaḥ tvām eva āśritya rāca aindra sadā dānava sattamāḥ nirbhayāḥ triṣu lokeṣu caranti icchā vihāriṇaḥ jāti mātram hi bhavataḥ hanti sarvān sadā hariḥ tena eva nirmitā māyā yayā saṃmohitaḥ bhavān bhavantam mohitam dṛṣṭvā randhra anveṣaṇa tatparaḥ bhavatām vijaya arthāya karoti indraḥ mahat tapaḥ imām māyā mayīm tyaktvā mantribhiḥ sahitaḥ bhavān gatvā haimavatam śailam pareṣām vighnam ācara mantri vṛddhān u pāhūya yathā vṛttāntam āha saḥ tat śrutvā nṛpatim prāha śrutavarmā vimṛśya ca ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇām rājyam tava śiva arpitam tasmāt api adhikam vīra gatam āsīt anekaśas aśakya pratikāryaḥ ayam yaḥ kālaśiva coditaḥ tava yuddhe mahā rāja parārtham bala hāriṇī dattā vidyā śivena eva tasmāt te vijayaḥ sadā anumene ca tad vākyam bhaṇḍaḥ dānava nāyakaḥ tapaḥ vighna karān dṛṣṭvā dānavān jagat aṃbikā tam dṛṣṭvā dānava indraḥ api kim etat iti vismitaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ dānava astreṇa babhañja atibalena tu vāyavya astreṇa tam dhīraḥ babhañja ca nanāda ca etat dṛṣṭvā tu daitya indraḥ viṣaṇmaḥ sva puram yayau tām ca dṛṣṭvā jagaddhātrīm dṛṣṭvā prākāram ujjvalam tān uvāca tatas śakraḥ daitya indraḥ ayam iha āgataḥ kuṇḍam yojana vistāram samyak kṛtvā tu śobhanam mahā yāga vidhānena praṇidhāya hutāśanam yajāmaḥ paramām śāktim mahā māsaiḥ vayam surāḥ brahma bhūtāḥ bhaviṣyāmaḥ bhokṣyāmaḥ vā triviṣṭapam huteṣu sarva māṃseṣu pādeṣu ca kareṣu ca jagat ujjīvana karīm brahma viṣṇu śiva ātmikām saundarya sāra sīmām tām ānanda rasa sāgarām japā kusuma saṃkāśām dāḍimī kusuma aṃbarām sarva ābharaṇa saṃyuktām śṛṅgāra eka rasa ālayām kṛpā taraṅgita apāṅga nayana āloka kaumudīm pāśa aṅkuśa ikṣu kodaṇḍa pañcabāṇa lasat karām tām vilokya mahādevīm devāḥ sarve sa vāsavāḥ praṇemuḥ mudita ātmānaḥ bhūyas bhūyas akhila ātmikam saṃpūrṇa aṅgāḥ dṛḍhatarāḥ vajra dehāḥ mahā balāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca mahā devīm aṃbikām akhila artha dām iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitopākhyāne lalitāprādurbhāvaḥ nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ jayakāri ca vāma akṣi jaya kāmākṣi sundari jaya akhila sura ārādhye jaya kāmeśi mānade jaya nārāyaṇi pare nandita aśeṣa viṣṭape jaya śrīkaṇṭha dayite jaya śrī lalitā iṃbike jātasya jāyamānasya iṣṭāpūrtasya hetave kalā muhūrta kāṣṭha ahar māsa ṛtu śarad ātmane rasātalam kaṭī deśaḥ kukṣiḥ te dharaṇī bhavet dṛśaḥ candra arka dahanāḥ diśaḥ te bāhavaḥ oṃbike marutaḥ tu tava ucchvāsāḥ vācaḥ te śrutayaḥ akhilāḥ krīḍā te loka racanā sakhā te cit mayaḥ śivaḥ āhāraḥ te sat ānandaḥ vāsaḥ te hṛdaye satām dṛśya adṛśya svarūpāṇi rūpāṇi bhuvanāni te śiroruhāḥ ghanāḥ te tu tārakāḥ kusumāni te yamāḥ ca niyamāḥ ca eva kara pāda ruhāḥ tathā prāṇāyāmaḥ tu te nāsā rasanā te sarasvatī pratyāhāraḥ tu idriṃyāṇi dhyānam te dhīḥ tu sattamā manaḥ te dhāraṇā śaktiḥ hṛdayam te samādhikaḥ mahīruhāḥ te iṅgaruhāḥ prabhātam vasanam tava yajñarūpā jagaddhātrī viśvarūpā ca pāvanī ādau yā tu dayā bhūtā sasarja nikhilāḥ prajāḥ hṛdaya sthā api lokānām adṛśyā mohana ātmikā nāma rūpa vibhāgam ca yā karoti sva līlayā tāni adhiṣṭhāya tiṣṭhantī teṣu asakta artha kāma dā yad ājñayā pravartante vahni sūrya aidumārutāḥ pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni tasyai devyai namaḥ namaḥ yā sasarja ādidhātāram sarga ādau ādi bhūri dam yathā dhṛtā tu dhariṇī yayā ākāśam ameyayā arūpam advandvam adṛṣṭa gocaram prabhāvam agryam katham aṃba varṇaye iti statvā mahādevīm devāḥ sarve sa vāsavāḥ bhūyas bhūyas namaskṛtya śaraṇam jagamuḥ añjasā tatas prasannā sā devī praṇatam vīkṣya vāsavam yadi tuṣṭā asi karyāṇi varam daitya indra pīḍitaḥ durdharam jīvitam dehi tvām gatāḥ śaraṇa arthinaḥ śrī devī uvāca nirbhayāḥ muditāḥ santu sarve deva gaṇāḥ tathā ye stoṣyanti ca mām bhaktyā stavena anena mānavāḥ bhājanam te bhaviṣyanti dharma śrī yaśasām sadā vidyā vinaya saṃpannāḥ nīrogāḥ dīrgha jīvinaḥ āmodam paramam jagmuḥ tām vilokya muhur muhur iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne lalitāstavarājaḥ nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ājagāma atha deveśīm draṣṭu kāmaḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ ājagāma tatas viṣṇuḥ ārūḍhaḥ vinatā sutam śivaḥ api vṛṣam ārūḍhaḥ samāyātaḥ akhila īśvarīm devarṣayaḥ nārada ādyāḥ samājagmuḥ maheśvarīm āyayuḥ tām mahā devīm sarve ca apsarasām gaṇāḥ viśvāvasu prabhṛtayaḥ gandharvāḥ ca eva yakṣakāḥ brahmaṇā atha samādiṣṭaḥ viśvakarmā viśām patiḥ cakāra nagaram divyam yathā amarapuram tathā vidyā adhidevatā śyāmā samājagmatuḥ aṃbikām mātaraḥ ca eva sva sva bhūta gaṇa āvṛtāḥ siddhayaḥ hi aṇima ādyāḥ ca yoginyaḥ ca eva koṭiśas bhairavāḥ kṣetrapālāḥ ca mahā śāstāḥ gaṇāgraṇīḥ āgatya te mahādevīm tuṣṭuvuḥ praṇatāḥ tadā tatra atha nagarīm ramyām sa aṭṭa prākāra toraṇām gaja aśva ratha śālā āḍhyām rāja vīthi virājitām sāmantānām amātyānām sainikānām dvijanma nām vetāla dāsa dāsīnām gṛhāṇi rucirāṇi ca madhyam rājagṛham divyam dvāra gopura bhūṣitam śālābhiḥ bahubhiḥ yuktam sabhābhiḥ uṣa śobhitam siṃhāsana sabhām ca eva nava ratna mayīm śubhām madhye siṃhāsanam divyam yaḥ tu etat samadhiṣṭhāya vartate bāliśaḥ api vā na kevalā strī rājya arhā puruṣaḥ api tayā vinā maṅgala ācārya saṃyuktam mahāpuruṣa lakṣaṇam anukūla aṅganā yuktam abhiṣiñcet iti śrutiḥ vibhāti iyam varārohā bhūrtā śṛṅgāradevatā varaḥ asyāḥ triṣu lokeṣu na ca anyaḥ śaṅkarāt ṛte jaḍilaḥ muṇḍadhārī ca virūpākṣaḥ kapālabhṛt kalmāṣī bhasma digdha aṅgaḥ śmaśāna asthi vibhūṣaṇaḥ amaṅgala āspadam ca enam varayet sā su maṅgalā koṭi kandarpa lāvaṇya yuktaḥ divya śarīravān kirīṭa hāra keyūra kuṇḍala ādyaiḥ alaṅkṛtaḥ tam kumāram atha āliṅgya brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ cakre kāmeśvaram nāmnā kamanīya vapuḥ dharam astuvan te parām śaktim brahma viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ tām dṛṣṭvā mṛgaśāvākṣīm kumāraḥ nīlalohitaḥ abhavat manmatha āviṣṭaḥ vismṛtya sakalāḥ kriyāḥ sā api tam vīkṣya tanu aṅgaḥ mūrtiṃmantam iva smaram madana āviṣṭa sarva aṅgī sva ātma rūpam amanyata athā uvāca mahādevīm brahmā loka eka nāyikām ime devāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ gandharva apsarasām gaṇāḥ tvām īśām draṣṭum icchanti sa priyām parama āhave loka saṃrakṣaṇa arthāya bhajasva puruṣam param rājñī bhava purasya asya sthitā bhava varāsane abhiṣiktām mahābhāgaiḥ devārṣe bhiḥ akalmaṣaiḥ sāmrājya cihna saṃyuktām sarva ābharaṇa saṃyutām sa priyām āsana gatām draṣṭum icchāmahe vayam iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalita upākhyāne madanakāmeśvaraprādurbhāvaḥ nāma caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca sa tatas vākyam brahma viṣṇu mukhān surān svatantrā aham sadā devāḥ sva icchā ācāra vihāriṇī uvāca ca mahādevīm dharma artha sahitam vacaḥ kāla krītā kraya krītā pitṛ dattā svayaṃyutā kāla krītā tu veśyā syāt kraya krītā tu dāsikā gandharva udvāhitā yuktā bhāryā syāt pitṛ dattakā samāna dharmiṇī yuktā bhāryā pitṛ vaśaṃvadā cit ānanda ātmakam tasmāt prakṛtiḥ samajāyata tvam eva anādiḥ akhilā kārya kāraṇa rūpiṇī tvām eva hi praśaṃsaṃti pañca brahma svarūpiṇīm tvām eva hi sṛjasi ādau tvam eva hi avasi kṣaṇāt bhajasva puruṣam kañcid loka anugraha kāmyayā iti vijñāpitā devī brahmaṇā sakalaiḥ suraiḥ tayā utsṛṣṭā hi sā mālā śobhayantī nabhasthalam papāta kaṇṭha deśe hi tadā kāmeśvarasya tu vavṛṣuḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi manda vāta īritāḥ ghanāḥ tvad rūpā hi mahādevī sahajaḥ ca bhavān api dātum arhasi kalyāṇīm asmai kāma śivāya tu dadau tasyai vidhānena prītyā tām śaṅkarāya tu deva ṛṣi pitṛ mukhyānām sarveṣām deva yoginām kalyāṇam kārayāmāsa śivayoḥ ādikeśavaḥ upāyanāni pradaduḥ sarve brahma ādayaḥ surāḥ tayoḥ puṣpāyudham prādāt amlānam hariḥ avyayam nāgapāśam dadau tābhyām varuṇaḥ yādasāṃpatiḥ aṅkuśam ca dadau tābhyām viśvakarmā viśām patiḥ kirīṭam agniḥ prāyacchat tāṭaṅkau candra bhāskarau nava ratna mayīm bhūṣām prādāt ratnākaraḥ svayam dadau surāṇām adhipaḥ madhu pātram atha akṣayam cintāmaṇi mayīm mālām kuberaḥ pradadau tadā sāmrājya sūcakam chatram dadau lakṣmīpatiḥ svayam gaṅgā ca yamunā tābhyām ca amare candra bhāsvare aṣṭau ca vasavaḥ rudrāḥ ādityāḥ ca aśvinau tathā dikpālāḥ marutaḥ sādhyāḥ gandharvāḥ pramatha īśvarāḥ svāni svāni āyudhāni asyai pradaduḥ paritoṣitāḥ rathān ca turagān nāgān mahā vegān mahā balān uṣṭān arogān aśvān tān kṣudh tṛṣṇā parivarjitān daduḥ vajra upama ākārān sa āyudhān sa paricchadān atha abhiṣekam ātenuḥ sāmrājye śivayoḥ śivam athā akarot vimānam ca nāmnā tu kusumākaram vidhātā a mlāna mālam vai nityam ca abhedyam āyudhaiḥ yat gandha ghrāṇa mātreṇa bhrānti roga kṣuḥ dhātayaḥ tad kṣaṇāt eva naśyanti manaḥ hlāda karam śubham vīṇā veṇu mṛdaṅga ādi vividhaiḥ taurya vādanaiḥ yayau vīthīm vihāra īśā śobhayantī nija ojasā sa lāja akṣata hastābhiḥ purandhrībhiḥ ca varṣitā gāthābhiḥ maṅgala arthābhiḥ vīṇā veṇu ādini svanaiḥ tuṣyantī vīvīthi vīthīṣu manda mandam atha āyayau pratigṛhya apsa robhiḥ tu kṛtam nīrājanā vidhim siṃhāsanam adhiṣṭhāya saha devena śaṃbhunā sarvajñā sa akṣipātena tat tat kāmān apūrayat tat dṛṣṭvā caritam devyāḥ brahmā loka pitāmahaḥ kāmākṣī iti tadā abhikhyām dadau kāmeśvarī iti ca vavarṣa āścarya meghaḥ api pure tasmin tad ājñayā mahārhāṇi ca vastūni divyāni ābharaṇāni ca cintāmaṇiḥ kalpavṛkṣaḥ kamalā kāmadhenavaḥ tām sevā eka rasa ākārām vimukta anya kriyā guṇāḥ sarva kāma artha saṃyuktāḥ hṛṣyantaḥ sārvakālikam pitāmahaḥ hariḥ ca eva mahādevaḥ ca vāsavaḥ anye diśām adhīśāḥ tu sakalāḥ devatā gaṇāḥ devarṣayaḥ nārada ādyāḥ sanaka ādyāḥ ca yoginaḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ ca manu ādyāḥ vaśiṣṭha ādyāḥ tapodhanāḥ gandharva apsarasaḥ yakṣāḥ yāḥ ca anyāḥ deva jātayaḥ divi bhūmi antarikṣeṣu sa saṃbādham vasaṃti ye toṣayāmāsa satatam anurāgeṇa bhūyasā rājñaḥ mahati bhūrloke viduṣaḥ sakala īpsitām rājñī dudoha abhīṣṭāni sarva bhū tala vāsinām triloka eka mahīpāle sa aṃbike kāma śaṅkare daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi yayuḥ kṣaṇaḥ iva aparaḥ tatas kadā cit āgatya nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ praṇamya paramām śaktim provāca vinaya anvitaḥ asat jana vināśa arthā sat jana abhyudaya arthinī pravṛttiḥ tava kalyāṇi sādhūnām rakṣaṇāya hi ayam bhaṇḍaḥ asuraḥ devi bādhate jagatām trayam tvad sevā eka parāḥ devāḥ cira kālam iha uṣitāḥ tvad ājñayā gamiṣyanti svāni svāni purāṇi tu amaṅgalāni śūnyāni samṛddha arthāni saṃtvataḥ evam vijñāpitā devī nāradena akhila īśvarī sva sva vāsa nivāsāya preṣayāmāsa ca amarān brahmāṇam ca harim śaṃbhum vāsava ādīn diśām patīn yathārham pūjayitvā tu preṣayāmāsa ca aṃbikā aparādham tatas tyaktum api saṃpreṣitāḥ surāḥ sva sva aṃśaiḥ śivayoḥ sevām ādi pitroḥ akurvata etat ākhyānam āyuṣyam sarva maṅgala kāraṇam āvirbhāvam mahādevyāḥ tasyāḥ rājya abhiṣecanam yaśaḥ prāpnoti vipulam samāna uttama tām api tāpa traya vihīnaḥ ca puruṣa arthaiḥ ca pūryate trisaṃdhyam yaḥ japet nityam dhyātvā siṃhāsana īśvarīm ṣaṣ māsāt mahatīm lakṣmīm prāpnuyāt jāpaka uttamaḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne vaivāhikotsavaḥ nāma pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha sā jagatām mātā lalitā parameśvarī trailokya kaṇṭakam bhaṇḍam daityam jetum viniryayau cakāra mardala ākārān aṃbhaḥ rāśīn tu sapta te prabhūta marddala dhvānaiḥ pūrayāmāsuḥ aṃbaram mṛdaṅga murajāḥ ca eva paṭahaḥ selukā jhallarī rāṅghā huhukā huṇḍukā ghaṭāḥ ānakāḥ paṇavāḥ ca eva gomukhāḥ ca ardhacandrikāḥ yava madhyāḥ muṣṭi madhyāḥ marddala aḍiṇḍimāḥ api jharjharāḥ ca barītāḥ ca iṅgya āliṅgya prabheda jāḥ uddhakāḥ caituhuṇḍāḥ ca niḥsāṇāḥ barbarāḥ pare huṅkārā kākatuṇḍāḥ ca vādya bhedāḥ tathā apare dadhvanuḥ śakti senābhiḥ āhatāḥ samara udyame lalitā parameśānyāḥ aṅkuśa astrān samudgatā saṃpatkarī nāma devī cacāla saha śaktibhiḥ aneka koṭi mātaṅga turaṅga ratha paṅktibhiḥ sevitā taruṇa ādityapāṭalā saṃpad īśvarī raṇa kolāhalam nāma sā āruroha mataṅga jam tām anvagāḥ yayau senā mahatī dhora rāviṇī lolābhiḥ ketu mālābhiḥ ullikhantī dhana adhanāt tasyāḥ ca saṃpad nāthāyāḥ pīna stana su saṃkaṭaḥ kaṇṭakaḥ ghana saṃnāhaḥ ruruce vakṣasi sthitaḥ kaṃpamānā khaḍga latā vyarucat tad kare dhṛtā kuṭilā kālanāthasya bhṛkuṭī iva bhayaṅkarā utpāta vāta saṃpātāt calitāḥ iva parvatāḥ tām anvagāḥ yayuḥ koṭi saṃkhyākāḥ kuñjara uttamāḥ atha śrī lalitā devyā śrī pāśa āyudha saṃbhavā ati tvarita vikrāntiḥ aśva ārūḍha acalat puraḥ tayā saha haya prāyam sainyam heṣā taraṅgitam vanāyu jāḥ ca kāṃbo jāḥ pāradāḥ siṃdhu deśa jāḥ ṭaṅkaṇāḥ parvatīyāḥ ca pārasīkāḥ tathā pare ajāneyāḥ ghaṭṭadharāḥ daradāḥ kāla vandijāḥ vālmīka yāvana udbhūtāḥ gāndharvāḥ ca atha ye hayāḥ prāc deśa jātāḥ kairātā prānta deśa udbhavāḥ tathā vinītāḥ sādhu voḍhāraḥ veginaḥ sthira cetasaḥ svāmi citta viśeṣa jñāḥ mahā yuddha sahiṣṇavaḥ lakṣaṇaiḥ bahubhiḥ yuktāḥ jita krodhāḥ jita śramāḥ pañca dhārāsu śakṣa ḍhyāḥ vinītāḥ ca plava anvitāḥ phala śukti śriyā yuktāḥ śveta śukti samanvitāḥ atha svastika śuktiḥ ca gaḍuram puṣpa gaṇḍikām etāni śubha lakṣmāṇi jya rājya pradāni ca vahantaḥ vāta javanāḥ vājinaḥ tām samanvayuḥ sthūla vāladhi vikṣepa kṣipyamāṇa payodharam jaṅghā kāṇḍa samunnaddha maṇi kiṅkiṇi bhāsuram vādayantam iva uccaṇḍaiḥ khura niṣṭhura kuṭṭanaiḥ bhū maṇḍala mahā vādyam vijayasya samṛddhaye ghoṣamāṇam prati muhur saṃdarśita gati kramam ālola cāmara vyājāt vahantam pakṣatī iva bhāṇḍaiḥ manoharaiḥ yuktam ghargharī jāla maṇḍitam eṣām ghoṣasya kapaṭāt huṅkurvatī imi vā asurān aśva ārūḍhā mahā devī samārūḍhā hayam yayau caturbhiḥ vāhubhiḥ pāśam aṅkuśam vetram eva ca taruṇa āditya saṅkāśā jvalat kāñcī taraṅgiṇī sañcacāla haya ārūḍhā nartayantī iva vājinam atha śrī daṇḍanāthāyāḥ niryāṇa paṭaha dhvaniḥ uddaṇḍa sindhu nisvānaḥ cakāra badhiram jagat vajra bāṇaiḥ kaṭhoraiḥ ca bhindantyaḥ kakubhaḥ daśa anyuddhata bhuja aśmānaḥ śaktayaḥ kāścid ucchritāḥ kāścid śrī daṇḍanāthāyāḥ khaḍgam phalakam ādāya pupluvuḥ caṇḍa saktayaḥ atyanta sainya sambādham vetra saṃtāḍanaiḥ śataiḥ atha tuṅga dhvaja śreṇīḥ mahiṣa aṅkāḥ mṛgāṅkikām siha aṅkāḥ ca eva bibhrāṇāḥ śaktayaḥ vyacalan purā tatas śrī daṇḍanāthāyāḥ śveta chatram sahasraśas sphurat karāḥ pracalitāḥ śaktayaḥ kāścid ādaduḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne sasenavijayayātrā nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ daṇḍanāthā viniryāṇe saṃkhyā atītaiḥ sita prabhaiḥ chatraiḥ gaganam āreje niḥsaṃkhyā śaśi maṇḍitam timiram nunude bhūyas tad kāṇḍa maṇi rociṣā vajra prabhā adhaga dhaga chāyā pūrita diṅmukhāḥ tālavṛntāḥ śatavidhāḥ kroḍa mukhyāḥ bale acalan caṇḍaḥ daṇḍa ādayaḥ tīvrā bhairavāḥ śula pāṇayaḥ jvalat keśā piśaṅga ābhāḥ taḍit bhāsura diṅmukhāḥ dahatyaḥ iva daitya oghān tīkṣṇaiḥ mārgaṇa vahnibhiḥ praceluḥ daṇḍanāthāyāḥ senāḥ nāsīra dhāvitāḥ atha potrī mukhī devī samāna ākṛti bhūṣaṇāḥ tad samāna āyudha karāḥ tad samāna sva vāhanāḥ tīkṣma daṃṣṭa viniṣṭhyūta vahri dhūma amita aṃbarāḥ tamāla śyāmala ākārāḥ kapilāḥ krūra locanāḥ sahasra mahiṣa ārūḍhāḥ praceluḥ sūkara ānanāḥ atha śrī daṇḍanāthā ca kari cakra ratha uttamāt vajraghoṣaḥ iti khyātam dhūta kesara maṇḍalam vyakta āsyam vikaṭa ākāram viśaṅkaṭa vilocanam daṃṣṭrā kaṭa kaṭatkāra badhirīkṛta diś taṭam vibantam iva bhū cakram āpātālam nimajjibhiḥ siṃhavāhanam āruhya vyacalat daṇḍanāyikā tasyām asura saṃhāre pravṛttāyām jvalat krudhi kim asau dhakṣyati ruṣā viśvam adyā eva potriṇī kim vā musala ghātena bhūmim dvedhā kariṣyati atha vā hala nirghātaiḥ kṣobhayiṣyati vāridhīn iti trasta hṛdaḥ sarve gagane nākinām gaṇāḥ dūra adrutam vimānaiḥ ca sa trāsam dadṛśuḥ gatāḥ vavandire ca tāḥ devāḥ baddhāñjali puṭa anvitāḥ kāni dvādaśa nāmāni tasyāḥ devyāḥ vada prabho aśva ānana mahā prājña yeṣu me kautukam mahat śṛṇu dvādaśa nāmāni tasyāḥ devyāḥ ghaṭodbhava yad ākarṇana mātreṇa prasannā sā bhaviṣyati pañcamī daṇḍanāthā ca saṃketā samayeśvarī tathā samayasaṃketā vārāhī potriṇī tathā vārtālī ca mahāsenā api ājñā cakreśvarī tathā arighnī ca iti samproktam nāma dvādaśakam mune saṃkaṭe duḥkham āpnoti na kadācana mānavaḥ etaiḥ nāmabhiḥ abhra sthāḥ saṃketām bahu tuṣṭuvuḥ teṣām anugraha arthāya pracacāla ca sā punar atha saṃketayoginyāḥ mantranāthā pada spṛśaḥ niryāṇa sūcana karī divi dadhvāna kāhalī śṛṅgāra prāya bhūṣāṇām śārdūla śyāmala tviṣām vīṇā saṃyata pāṇīnām śaktīnām niryayau balam kāścad gāyanti nṛtyanti matta kokila niḥsvanāḥ vīṇā veṇu mṛdaṅga ādyāḥ savilāsa padakramāḥ praceluḥ śaktayaḥ śyāmāḥ harṣayantyaḥ jagat janān mayūra vāhanāḥ kāścid katicid haṃsa vāhanāḥ katicid nakula ārūḍhāḥ katicid kokila āsanāḥ sarvāḥ ca śyāmala ākārāḥ kāścid karṇīratha sthitāḥ kādaṃba madhu mattāḥ ca kāścid ārūḍha saindhavāḥ mantranāthām puraskṛtya saṃpraceluḥ puras puras bāla arka varṇa kavacā mada ālola vilocanā īṣat prasveda kaṇikā manohara mukha aṃbujā prekṣayantī kiñcid bhrū valli tāṇḍavaiḥ āsām madhye na ca anyāsām śaktīnām ujjvala udayā nirjagāma ghana śyāma śyāmalā mantranāyikā tām tuṣṭuvuḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ nāmabhiḥ nāka vāsinaḥ tāni ṣoḍaśa nāmāni śṛṇu kuṃbha samudbhava saṃgītayoginī śyāmā śyāmalā mantranāyikā mantriṇī saciva īśī ca pradhāna īśī śukapriyā vīṇāvatī vaiṇikī ca mudriṇī priyakapriyā nipapriyā kadaṃbeśī kadaṃba vana vāsinī sadāmadā ca nāmāni ṣoḍaśa etāni kuṃbha ja etaiḥ yaḥ saciva īśānīm sakṛt stauti śarīravān lalitā parameśānyāḥ rājya carcā tu yāvatī śaktīnām api carcā yā sā sarvatra jaya pradā atha saṃgīta yoginyāḥ kara sthāt śu kapotakāt namaskṛtya pradhāna īśīm idam āha sa bhaktimān catrajīvam imam nāma kodaṇḍam su mahattaram gṛhāṇa jagatām aṃba dānavānām nibarhaṇam imau ca akṣaya bāṇa āḍhyau tūṇīrau svarṇa citritau gṛhāṇa daitya nāśāya mama anugraha hetave arpitān cāpa tūṇīrān jagrāha priyaka priyā citrajīvam mahā cāpam ādāya ca śūkapriyā visphāram janayāmāsa maurvīm udvādya bhūriśas saṃgīta yoginī cāpa dhvaninā pūritam jagat nāka ālayānām ca manona yana ānanda saṃpadā yantriṇī ca iti dve tasyāḥ paricārike śukam vīṇām ca sahasā vahantyau pariceratuḥ ālola valaya kvāṇa vardhiṣṇu guṇa nisvanam dhārayantī ghanaśyāmā cakāra ati manoharam citrajīva śarāsena bhūṣitā gītayoginī kālī kaṭākṣa vat tīkṣṇaḥ nṛtyat bhujaga bhīṣaṇaḥ ullasan dakṣiṇe pāṇau vilalāsa śilīmukhaḥ geya cakra ratha ārūḍhām tām paścāt ca siṣevire tadvat śyāmala śobhā āḍhyāḥ devyaḥ bāṇa dhanuḥ dharāḥ sahasra akṣauhiṇī saṃkhyāḥ tīvra vegāḥ mada alasāḥ āpūrayantyaḥ kakubham kalaiḥ kilikilā ravaiḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne daṇḍanāthāśyāmalāsenāyātrā nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha rāja nāyikā śritā ājvalita aṅkuśā phaṇi samāna pāśa bhṛt daśa yojana āyati mātā jagat trayīm abhivṛṇvatā viśada mauktika ātmanā dhavala ātapatra valayena bhāsurā śaśi maṇḍalasya sakhitām upeyuṣā abhivījitā ca maṇi kānta śobhinā vijaya ādi mukhya paricārikā gaṇaiḥ śaktyā eka rājya padavīm abhisūcayantī sāmrājya cihna śata maṇḍita sainya deśā saṃgīta vādya racanā abhiratha amarīṇām saṃstūyamāna vibhavā viśada prakāśā ābaddha bhakti vipula añjali śekharāṇām ārāt ahaṃprathamikā kṛta sevanānām brahma īśa viṣṇu vṛṣa mukhya sura uttamānām vaktrāṇi varṣita nutīni kaṭākṣayantī kāmeśvarī prabhṛtibhiḥ kamanīya bhābhiḥ saṃgrāma veṣa racanā su manoharābhiḥ tīvrābhiḥ rāvaṇa suśakti paraṃparabhiḥ yuktam ratham samara karmaṇi cālayantī prodyat piśaṅga ruci bhāga mala aṃśukena vīta amanohara ruciḥ samare vyabhāsīt pañca adhikaiḥ viśati nāma ratnaiḥ prapañca pāpa praśama ati dakṣaiḥ saṃstūyamānā lalitā marudbhiḥ saṃgrāmam uddiśya samuccacāla vījivaktra mahābuddhe pañcaviṃśati nāmabhiḥ lalitā parameśānyāḥ dehi karṇa rasāyanam sundarī cakranāthā ca sāmrājī cakriṇī tathā cakreśvarī mahādevī kāmeśī parameśvarī mahāvidyā śivā anaṅgavallabhā sarvapāṭalā kula nāthā āmnāya nāthā sarva āmnāya nivāsinī śṛṅgāranāyikā ca iti pañcaviṃśati nāmabhiḥ stuvanti ye mahābhāgām lalitām parameśvarīm te prāpnuvanti saubhāgyam aṣṭau siddhīḥ mahat yaśaḥ ittham pracaṇḍa saṃraṃbham cālayantī mahat balam bhaṇḍāsuram prati kruddhā cacāla lalitā aṃbikā iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne lalitā parameśvarī senā jaya yātrā nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ cakrarāja ratha indrasya yāḥ parvaṇi samāśritāḥ devatāḥ prakaṭa abhikhyāḥ tāsām ākhyām nivedaya saṃkhyāḥ ca tāsām akhilāḥ varṇa bhedān ca śobhanān proktāḥ siddhidevyaḥ tāsām nāmāni mat śṛṇu aṇimā mahimā ca eva laghimā garimā tathā īśitā pūrṇāḥ yogibhiḥ ca niṣevitāḥ tatra pūrva arddha bhāge ca brahma ādyāḥ aṣṭa śaktayaḥ brāhmī māheśvarī ca eva kaumārī vaiṣmavī tathā vārāhī ca eva māṃhendrī cāmuṇḍā ca eva saptamī mahā lakṣmīḥ aṣṭamī ca dvi bhujāḥ śoṇa vigrahāḥ kapālam utpalam ca eva bibhrāṇāḥ rakta vāsasaḥ atha vā anya prakāreṇa kecid dhyānam pacakṣate brahma ādi sadṛśa ākārāḥ brahma ādi sadṛśa āyudhāḥ brahma ādīnām param cihnam dhārayantyaḥ prakīrtitāḥ tāsām ūrdhva sthāna gatām mudrāḥ devyaḥ mahattarāḥ dāḍimī puṣpa saṅkāśāḥ pīta aṃbara manoharāḥ catur bhujāḥ bhuja dvandva dhṛta carma kṛpāṇakāḥ mada rakta vilola akṣyaḥ tāsām nāmāni mat śṛṇu sarva saṃkṣobhiṇī ca eva sarva vidrāviṇī tathā sarva ākarṣaṇa kṛt mudrā tathā sarva vaśaṅkarī sarva unmādana mudrā ca yaṣṭiḥ sarva mahā aṅkuśā sarvakhecarikā mudrā sarvabījā tathā aparā sarvayoniḥ ca navamī tathā sarvatriśaṇḍikā siddhi brāha yādi mudrāḥ tāḥ etāḥ prakaṭa śaktayaḥ bhaṇḍa asurasya saṃhāram kartum rakta rathe sthitāḥ yāḥ guptā ākhyāḥ pūrvam uktāḥ tāsām nāmāni mat śṛṇu kāma ākarṣaṇikā ca eva buddhi ākarṣaṇikā kalā ahaṅkāra ākarṣiṇī ca śabda ākarṣaṇikā kalā sparśa ākarṣaṇikā nityā rūpa ākarṣaṇikā kalā rasa ākarṣaṇikā nityā gandha ākarṣaṇikā kalā citta ākarṣaṇikā nityā dhairya ākarṣaṇikā kalā smṛtyā karṣaṇikā nityā nāma ākarṇaṇikā kalā bīja ākarṣaṇikā nityā ca ātma karṣaṇikā kalā amṛta ākarṣaṇī nityā śarīra ākarṣiṇī kalā etāḥ ṣoḍaśa śītāṃśu kalā rūpāḥ ca śaktayaḥ aṣṭamam parva samprāptāḥ guptāḥ nāmnā prakīrtitāḥ vidruma druma saṅkāśāḥ mandasmita manoharāḥ cāpa bāṇau carma khaḍgau dadhānāḥ divya kāntayaḥ bhaṇḍa asura vadha arthāya pravṛttāḥ kumbhasambhava saptame parvaṇi kṛta āvāsāḥ guptatara abhidhāḥ anaṅga madana anaṅgamadana āturayā saha anaṅgalekhā ca anaṅgavegā anaṅgāṅkuśā api ca anaṅgam āligya aparāḥ etāḥ devyaḥ japā tviṣaḥ ikṣu kṛta kaca stomāḥ siṃdūra tilaka ujjvalāḥ ati tīvra svabhāvāḥ ca kāla anala sama tviṣaḥ vahnibāṇam vahnicāpam vahni rūpam asim tathā vahni cakra ākhyā phalakam dadhānāḥ dīpta vigrahāḥ ājñā śaktayaḥ eva etāḥ lalitāyāḥ mahā ojasaḥ sarva saṃkṣobhiṇī ca eva sarva vidrāviṇī tathā sarva ākarṣaṇikā śaktiḥ sarva āhlādinikā tathā sarva jṛṃbhaṇa śaktiḥ ca sarva unmādana śaktikā evam tu sampradāyānām nāmāni kathitāni vai atha pañcama parva sthāḥ kula uttīrṇāḥ iti smṛtāḥ tāḥ ca saptaṭika saṅkāśāḥ paraśum pāśam eva ca gadām ghaṇṭām maṇim ca eva dadhānāḥ dīpta vigrahāḥ deva dviṣam ati kruddhāḥ bhrukuṭī cakre turīya parva sthāḥ muktā hāra sama tviṣaḥ nigarbha yoginī nāmnā prathitāḥ daśa kīrtitāḥ sarvajñā sarva śaktiḥ ca sarva aiśvarya pradā tathā sarva jñāna mayī devī sarva vyādhi vināśinī sarva uṅgam kṛpāṇikām tisraḥ tripīṭha nilayāḥ aṣṭa bāhu samanvitāḥ palakam nāgapāśam ca ghaṇṭām ca eva mahā dhvanim vibhrāṇāḥ madirā mattāḥ ati gupta rahasyakāḥ kāmeśī ca eva vajreśī bhagamālinī atha aparā tisraḥ etāḥ smṛtāḥ devyaḥ bhaṇḍe kopa samanvitāḥ lalitā sama māhātmyāḥ lalitā sama tejasaḥ etāḥ tu nityam śrī devyāḥ antaraṅgāḥ prakīrtitāḥ paritas racita āvāsāḥ proktāḥ pañcadaśa akṣarāḥ tithi nityāḥ kastūrī tilaka ullāsi bhālā muktā virājitāḥ kavaca channa sarva aṅgāḥ palāśa prasava tviṣaḥ pañca kāmāḥ ime proktāḥ bhaṇḍa asura vadha arthinaḥ brahmī mukhyāḥ tu pūrva uktāḥ caṇḍikā tu aṣṭamī parā eva ca etāḥ tu kuravinda ābhāḥ jagat kṣobhaṇa laṃpaṭāḥ mahā sarasam annāham ādadhānāḥ pade pade vajra kaṅkaṭa saṃchannāḥ aṭṭahāsa ujjvalāḥ pare vajra daṇḍau śataghnīm ca saṃbibhrāṇāḥ bhuśuṇḍikāḥ atha yakṣaḥ somaḥ yakṣeśvaraḥ tathā īśānaḥ ca jagat cakra bhakṣakaḥ śūla bhīṣaṇaḥ brahmā ca eva aśvinī putraḥ vaidya vidyā viśāradau dhanvantariḥ ca bhagavān atha anye gaṇanāyakāḥ kaṭa kāṇḍa galat dāna saṃtarpita madhu vratāḥ mahāpadmaḥ śaṅkhapālaḥ gulikaḥ subalaḥ tathā ete nāga īśvarāḥ ca eva nāga koṭibhiḥ āvṛtāḥ pūrva ādi diśam ārabhya paritas kṛta mandirāḥ tatra eva devatāḥ cakre cakra ākārāḥ marut diśaḥ āśritya kila vartante tad adhiṣṭhātṛ devatāḥ jṛṃbhiṇī staṃbhinī ca eva mohinī tisraḥ eva ca kapālam ca gadām bibhrat ūrdhva keśaḥ mahā vapuḥ pātāla tala jaṃbāla bahulā kāra kālimā aṭṭahāsa mahā vajra dīrṇa brahmāṇḍa maṇḍalaḥ phūtkārī tripurā yuktam phaṇi pāśam kare vahan kṣetrapālaḥ sadā bhāti sevamānaḥ kiṭīśvarīm ruhya pravavṛte bhaṇṭā sura badha eṣiṇī prāk uktam eva deveśī vāha siṃhasya lakṣaṇam tasya eva parvaṇaḥ adhastāt daṇḍanāthā sama tviṣaḥ daṇḍinī sadṛśa aśeṣa bhūṣaṇa āyudha maṇḍitāḥ śamyāḥ kroḍa ānanāḥ candra rekhā uttaṃsita kuntalāḥ lalitā drohiṇām śyāmā drohiṇām svāminī druhām nija bhakta droha kṛtāḥ mantra mālā vibhūṣaṇāḥ sva goṣṭhī samāyā kṣepa kāriṇām muṇḍa maṇḍalaiḥ sahasram devatāḥ proktāḥ sevamānāḥ kiṭīśvarīm tāsām nāmāni sarvāsām daṇḍinyāḥ kuṃbha saṃbhava sahasranāma adhyāye tu vakṣyante na adhunā punar atha tāsām devatānām kolāsyānām samīpatas vāhanam kṛṣṇasāraṅgaḥ daṇḍinyāḥ samaye sthitaḥ krośa ardha ardha āyataḥ śṛṅge tad ardha ardha āyataḥ mukhe sadā ca uddhṛta vāladhiḥ udare dhavala chāyaḥ huṅkāreṇa mahīyasā varttate madirā siṃdhuḥ devatā rūpam āsthitā māṇikya giri vat śoṇam haste piśita piṇḍakam dadhānā na akṣī hema aṃbhoja sraj āvṛtā mada śaktyā samāśliṣṭā dhṛta rakta sarojayā yadā yadā saṃgrāme saṃpravartate yuddha sveda manuprāptāḥ śaktayaḥ syuḥ pipāsitāḥ tadā tadā surā siṃdhuḥ ātmānam bahudhā kṣipan raṇe khedam devatānām añjasā apākariṣyati tadā śroṣyasi saṃgrāme kathyamānam mayā mudā upari api kṛta āvāsāḥ hetuka ādyāḥ daśa smṛtāḥ mahāntaḥ bhairava śreṣṭhāḥ khyātāḥ vipula vikramāḥ tejobhiḥ ddivā dīpita bhānavaḥ kalpa anta kāle daṇḍinyā ājñayā viśva ghasmarāḥ ati udagra prakṛtayaḥ rada daṣṭa oṣṭha saṃpuṭāḥ triśūla agra vinirbhinna mahā vārida maṇḍalāḥ hetukaḥ tripurāriḥ ca tṛtīyaḥ ca agnibhairavaḥ bhīma rūpaḥ hāṭakeśaḥ tathā eva acala nāmavān ete daśa eva vikhyātāḥ daśa koṭi bhaṭa anvitāḥ evam hi daṇḍanāthāyāḥ kiri cakrasya devatāḥ jṛṃbhiṇī ādi acala indra antāḥ proktāḥ trailokya pāvanāḥ dānavāḥ mārayiṣyante pāsyante rakta vṛṣṭayaḥ ittham bahuvidha trāṇam parva sthaiḥ devatā gaṇaiḥ kiri cakram daṇḍa netryāḥ ratha ratnam cacāla ha śakti senā sahasrasya antar cacāra tadā śubham mahā ghoṣaḥ pravavṛte śaktīnām sainya maṇḍale lalitā cakrarāja ākhyā rathanāthasya kīrtitāḥ ṣaṣ sārathayaḥ uddaṇḍa pāśa grahaṇa kovidāḥ sārasaḥ pañcamaḥ ca eva cāmuṇḍā ca tathā parā etāsu devatāḥ tatra ratha sārathayaḥ smṛtāḥ tat eva śakti sāmrājya sūcakam parikīrtitam atha sā lalitā īśānī sarva śakti maheśvarī mahā sāmrājya padavīm ārūḍhā parameśvarī cacāla bhaṇḍadā iti asya kṣaya siddhi abhikāṅkṣiṇī śabdāyante diśaḥ sarvāḥ kaṃpate ca vasuṃdharā deva dundubhayaḥ neduḥ nipetuḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭayaḥ viśvāvasu prabhṛtayaḥ gandharvāḥ sura gāyakāḥ tumburuḥ nāradaḥ ca eva sākṣāt eva sarasvatī jaya maṅgala padyāni paṭhantaḥ paṭu gītibhiḥ harṣa saṃphulla vadanāḥ sphurat pulaka bhūṣaṇāḥ harṣeṇa āḍhyāḥ mada unmattāḥ pranṛtyantaḥ pade pade saptarṣayaḥ vasiṣṭha ādyāḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāma rūpibhiḥ haviṣā iva mahā vahni śikhām atyanta pāvinīm āśīrvādena mahatā vardhayāmāsuḥ uttamāḥ taiḥ stūyamānā lalitā rājamānā ratha uttame bhaṇḍa asuram vinirjetum uddaṇḍaiḥ saha sainikaiḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalita upākhyāne kiricakrarathadevatāprakāśanam nāma viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ākarṇya lalitā devyāḥ yātrā nigama nisvanam mahāntam kṣobham āyātāḥ bhaṇḍa asura pura ālayāḥ viṣaṅga agraja daityasya sadā āvāsaḥ kila abhavat vitresuḥ surāḥ sarve śrī devī āgama saṃbhramāt śata yojana vistīrṇam tat sarvam puram āsuram dhūmaiḥ iva āvṛtam abhūt utpāta janitaiḥ muhur dhūrṇamānā patanti sma mahā ulkāḥ gagana sthalāt utpātānām prāthamikaḥ bhūkaṃpaḥ paryavartata dhvaja agra vartinaḥ kaṅka gṛdhrāḥ ca eva bakāḥ khagāḥ āditya maṇḍale dṛṣṭvā a dṛṣṭvā cakranduḥ uccakais muhur ākāśa vāṇībhiḥ paruṣābhiḥ babhāṣire sarvatas dikṣu dṛśyante ketavaḥ tu malīmasāḥ dhūmāyamānāḥ prakṣobha janakāḥ daitya rakṣasām daitya strīṇām ca vibhraṣṭāḥ akāle bhūṣaṇa srajaḥ hāhā iti dūram krandantyaḥ paryaśru samarodiṣuḥ dapaṇānām varmaṇām ca dhvajānām khaḍga saṃpadām maṇīnām aṃbarāṇām ca mālinyam abhavat muhur saudheṣu candraśālāsu keli veśmasu sarvatas aṭṭālakeṣu goṣṭheṣu vipaṇeṣu sabhāsu ca catuṣkikāsu aliṅgeṣu pragrīveṣu valeṣu ca svastikeṣu ca sarveṣu garbhāgāra puṭeṣu ca gopureṣu kapāṭeṣu valabhīnām ca sīmasu vātāyaneṣu kakṣyāsu dhiṣṇyeṣu ca khaleṣu ca aśrūyanta mahā ghoṣāḥ paruṣāḥ bhūta bhāṣitāḥ śithilī savatas jātā ghora parṇā bhayānakā karaṭaiḥ kaṭuka ālāpaiḥ valoki divākaraḥ ārāviṣu karoṭīnām koṭayaḥ ca apatan bhuvi apatan vedi madhyeṣu bindavaḥ śoṇita aṃbhasām keśa oghakāḥ ca niṣpetuḥ sarvatas dhūma dhūsarāḥ bhauma āntarikṣa divyānām utpātānām iti vrajam avalokya bhṛśam trastāḥ sarve nagara vāsinaḥ nivedayāmāsuḥ amī bhaṇḍāya prathita ojase sa ca bhaṇḍaḥ pracaṇḍa utthaiḥ taiḥ utpāta kadaṃbakaiḥ asaṃjāta dhṛti bhraṃśaḥ mantra sthānam upāgamat sphurat mukuṭa lagnānām ratnānām kiraṇaiḥ ghanaiḥ dīpayan akhila aśāntān adyutat dānava īśvaraḥ tuṅga siṃhāsana stham tam siṣevāte tadā tathā api eṣā na avamānyā kadācana alpaḥ api ripuḥ ātma jñaiḥ na avamānyaḥ jigīṣubhiḥ tasmāt tad utsāraṇa artham preṣaṇīyāḥ tu kiṅkarāḥ sa kaca graham ākṛṣya sā a netavyā mada uddhatā deva tvadīya saha bala utkaṭaiḥ atha bhaṇḍāsuḥ ājñaptaḥ kuṭilākṣaḥ mahā balaḥ rakṣaṇa artham daśa akṣau hiṇī upetam tālajaṅghakam avācīne pura dvāre daśa akṣauhiṇikā yutam nāmnā tālabhujam daityam rakṣaṇa artham akalpayat pratīcīne pura dvāre daśa akṣauhiṇikā yutam tālagrīvam nāma daityam rakṣā artham samakalpayat ādideśa sa rakṣā artham daśa akṣauhiṇikā yutam maṇḍala ākārataḥ vastun daśākṣauhiṇim ādiśat evam pañcāśatā kṛtvā akṣauhiṇyā pura rakṣaṇam kuṭilākṣaḥ uvāca deva tvad ājñayā dattam sainyam nagara rakṣaṇe durmadaḥ preṣitaḥ pūrvam duṣṭām tām lalitām prati asmad kiṅkara mātreṇa su nirāśā hi sā abalā tathā api rājñām ācāraḥ karttavyam pura rakṣaṇam iti uktvā bhaṇḍa daitya indram kubila akṣaḥ ati garvitaḥ dūtaḥ tu preṣitaḥ pūrvam kuṭilākṣeṇa dānavaḥ kṛtvā kilakilā rāvam bhaṭāḥ tatra sahasraśas tāḥ ca śaktyaḥ uddaṇḍāḥ sphurita aṭṭahasa svanāḥ dedīpyamāna śastra ābhāḥ samayudhyanta dānavaiḥ śaktīnām dānavānām ca saṃśobhita jagattrayaḥ samavartata saṃgrāmaḥ dhūli grāma tata ambaraḥ ratha vaṃśeṣu mūrcchantyaḥ kari kaṇṭhaiḥ prapañcitāḥ aśva niḥśvāsa vikṣiptāḥ dhūlayaḥ ravam prapedire tam āpatantam ālokya daśa akṣauhiṇikā vṛtam sampatkarī samānābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ samadhiṣṭhitāḥ aśvāḥ ca dantinaḥ mattāḥ vyamardan dānatrīm camum dhūlīṣu dhūyamānāsu tāḍyamānāsu bheriṣu śaktibhiḥ pātyamānānām dānavānām sahasraśas dhvajāni luṭhitāni āsan vilūnāni śilīmukhaiḥ rakta aruṇāyām yuddha urvyām patitaiḥ chatra maṇḍalaiḥ ālaṃbi tulanā saṃdhyā rakta abhra hima rociṣā jvālā kapālaḥ kalpa agniḥ iva cāru payonidhau daitya sainyāni nivahāḥ śaktīnām paryavārayan dānavānām raṇa tale nipetuḥ muṇḍa rāśayaḥ daṣṭa oṣṭhaiḥ bhrukuṭī krūraiḥ krodha saṃrakta locanaiḥ muṇḍaiḥ akhaṇḍam abhavat saṃgrāma dharaṇī talam itas tatas śakti śastraiḥ tāḍitāḥ mūrcchitāḥ iti vineśuḥ dānavāḥ tatra saṃpad devī bala āhatāḥ atha bhagnam samāśvāsya nijam balam arindamaḥ dīrgha grīvaḥ samunnaddhaḥ pṛṣṭhe niṣṭhura todanaḥ adhiṣṭhitaḥ durmadena vāhana uṣṭraḥ cacāla ha tam uṣṭra vāhanam duṣṭam anvīyuḥ kruddha cetasaḥ dānau anaśvasat sarvān bhītān śakti yuyutsayā saṃpad karīcamū cakram vanam vārbhiḥ iva aṃbudaḥ tena duḥsaha sattvena tāḍitāḥ bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ staṃbhitā iva abhavat senā saṃpad karyāḥ kṣaṇam raṇe atha krodha aruṇam cakṣuḥ dadhānā saṃpad aṃbikā raṇa kolāhala gajam ārūḍhā ayudhyata amunā ālola kaṅkaṇa kvāṇa ramaṇīyataraḥ karaḥ tasyāḥ ca ākṛṣya kodaṇḍa maurvīm ākarṇam āhave laghu hasta tayā apaśyan ākṛṣṭat na ca mokṣaṇam dadṛśe ghanuṣaḥ cakram kevalam śara dhāraṇe āśu arka abara saṃparka sphuṭa pratiphalat phalāḥ śarāḥ sampad karī cāpa cyutāḥ samadahan arīn abhūt anyonya saṃghaṭṭāt visphuliṅga śilīmukhaiḥ prathamam prasṛtaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sampad devī suradviṣoḥ tad antare ca bāṇānām ati saṃghaṭṭa yonayaḥ tayā adhirūḍhaḥ saṃśroṇyā araṇa kolāhalaḥ karī parākramam bahuvidham darśayāmāsa saṃgare kareṇa katicid daityān pāda ghātena kāṃścana udagra danta musala ghātaiḥ anyān ca dānavān vāla kāṇḍa hataiḥ anyān phetkāraiḥ aparān ripūn pṛthu māna abhighātena kāṃścid daityan vyamardayat caturam caritam cakre saṃpad devī mataṅga jaḥ su durmadaḥ krudhā raktaḥ dṛḍhena ekena patriṇā saṃpad karī mukuṭa gam maṇim ekam apāharat atha krodha aruṇa dṛśā tayā muktaiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ vikṣataḥ vakṣasi kṣipram durmadaḥ jīvitam jahau tatas kilakilā rāvam kṛtvā śakti camū varaiḥ hata avaśiṣṭāḥ daityāḥ tu śakti bāṇaiḥ khilīkṛtāḥ palāyitāḥ raṇa kṣoṇyāḥ śūnyakam puram āśrayan tad vṛttāntam atha ākarṇya saṃkruddhaḥ dānava īśvaraḥ pracaṇḍena prabhāveṇa dīpyamānaḥ iva ātmani kuṭila akṣam nikaṭa gam babhāṣe pṛtanāpatim katham sā duṣṭa vanitā durmadam bala śālinam nipātitavatī yuddhe kaṣṭaḥ eva vidheḥ kramaḥ tām duṣṭa vanitām jetum ākraṣṭum ca kacam haṭhāt senāpatim kuraṇḍa ākhyam preṣaya āhava durmadam eti saṃproṣitaḥ tena kuṭila akṣaḥ mahā palam kuraṇḍam caṇḍa dos daṇḍam ājuhāva prabhoḥ puras sa kuraṇḍaḥ samāgatya praṇāma svāmine adiśat uvāca kuṭila akṣaḥ tam gaccha sajjaya sainikān māyāyām caturaḥ asi tvam citra yuddha viśārada kūṭa yuddhe ca nipuṇaḥ tām striyam parimardaya iti svāmi puraḥ tena kuṭilākṣeṇa deśitaḥ nirjagāma purāt tūrṇam kuraṇḍaḥ caṇḍa vikramaḥ viṃśati akṣauhiṇībhiḥ ca samantāt parivāritaḥ durmadasya agrajaḥ caṇḍaḥ kuraṇḍaḥ samaram yayau dūlībhiḥ tumulīkurvan digantam dhīra mānasaḥ śārṅgam dhanuḥ samādāya ghora ṭaṅkāram utsvanam vavarṣa śara dhārabhiḥ saṃpatkaryā mahā camūm vṛthā vahasi vikrānti lava leśam mahā madam idānīm ca eva bhavatīm etaiḥ nārāca maṇḍalaiḥ antakasya purīm atra prāpayiṣyāmi paśya mām apūrvam aṅganā raktam pibantu raṇapūtanāḥ sainyam protsāhayāmāsa śakti senā vimardane atha tām pṛtanām caṇḍī kuraṇḍasya mahā ojasaḥ apurva āhava saṃjāta kautukā atha jagāda tām aśva rūḍhā samāgatya sa sneha ārdram idam vacaḥ sakhi saṃpatkari prītyā mama vāṇī yācitā asi sakhi tvena na atra saṃśayam ācara iti tasyāḥ vacaḥ śrutvā saṃpad devyā śuci smitā nivartayāmāsa camūm kuruṇḍa abhimukha utthitām atha bāla arka varṇābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ samadhiṣṭhitāḥ taraṅgāḥ iva sainya abdheḥ turaṅgāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ kharaiḥ khura puṭaiḥ kṣoṇīm ullikhantaḥ muhur muhur ghati bhedeṣu cāreṣu pañcadhā khura pātane protsāhane ca saṃjñābhiḥ kara pāda agra yonibhiḥ caturābhiḥ turaṅgasya hṛdaya jñābhiḥ āhave aśva ārūḍha aṃbikā sainya śaktibhiḥ saha dānavāḥ protsāhitāḥ kuraṇḍena samayudhyanta durmadāḥ evam pravṛtte samare śaktīnām ca suradviṣām abhyadravat durācāram aśva ārūḍhāḥ kuraṇḍakam saṃdhyā anurakta śītāṃśu maṇḍalī suṃdara ānanā smayamānā iva samare gṛhīta maṇi kārmukā avākirat śara āsāraiḥ kuraṇḍam turaga ānanā turaga ārūḍhayā utkṣiptāḥ samākrāman digantarān diśaḥ daśa vyānaśire rukma puṅkhāḥ śilīmukhāḥ durmadasya agrajaḥ kruddhaḥ kuraṇḍaḥ caṇḍa vikramaḥ viśikhaiḥ śārṅga niṣṭhyūtaiḥ aśva ārūḍhā mavākirat caṇḍaiḥ khura puṭaiḥ sainyam khaṇḍayan ati vegataḥ aśva ārūḍha aturaṅgaḥ api mardayāmāsa dānavān tasyāḥ heṣā ravāt dūram utpāta aṃbudhi niḥsvanaḥ amūrcchayan anekāni tasya ānītāni vairiṇaḥ nijam pāśa āyudham divyam mumoca jvalita ākṛti tasmāt pāśāt koṭiśas anye pāśāḥ bhujaga bhīṣaṇāḥ chinnam aurvi dhanuḥ tyaktvā bhṛśam kruddhā haya āsanā aṅkuśam pātayāmāsa tasya vakṣasi durmateḥ tena aṅkuśena jvalatā pīta jīvita śoṇitaḥ tad aṅkuśa viniṣṭhyūtāḥ putanāḥ kāścid udbhaṭāḥ tat sainyam pāśa nisyandam bhakṣayitvā kṣayam gatāḥ ittham kuruṇḍe nihate viṃśati akṣauhiṇī patau hata avaśiṣṭāḥ te daityāḥ prapalāyanta vai drutam kuraṇḍam sa anujam yuddhe śakti sainyaiḥ nipātitam śrutvā śūnyaka nāthaḥ api niśaśvāsa bhujaṅga vat iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne durmadakuraṇḍavadhaḥ nāma dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha aśva rūḍhayā kṣipte kuraṇḍe bhaṇḍa dānavaḥ yat ca no śaṅkitam citte tat etat kaṣṭam āgatam duṣṭa dāsyāḥ prabhāvaḥ ayam māyāvinyāḥ mahattaraḥ itas param karaṅka ādīn pañca senā adhināyakān śatam akṣauhiṇīnām ca prasthāpaya raṇa aṅgaṇe te yuddha durmadāḥ śūrāḥ saṃgrāmeṣu tanutyajaḥ iti bhaṇḍa vacaḥ śrutvā bhṛśam catvarayā anvitaḥ kuṭilākṣaḥ karaṅka ādīn ājuhāva camūpatīn te svāminam namaskṛtya kuṭilākṣeṇa deśitāḥ teṣām prayāṇa niḥsāṇa raṇitam bhṛśa duḥsaham ākarṇya diggajāḥ tūrṇam śīrṇa karṇāḥ jughūrṇire śatam akṣauhiṇīnām ca prācalat ketumālakam hreṣamāṇa haya ākīrṇam krandat bhaṭa kula udbhavam bṛṃhamāṇa gajam garjat ratha yakram cacāla tat cakranemi hata kṣoṇī reṇu kṣapita rociṣā dhūlī mayam iva aśeṣam abhavat viśva maṇḍalam udbhūtaiḥ dhūlikā jālaiḥ ākrāntāḥ daitya sainikāḥ iyattayā atas senāyāḥ saṃkhyā api paribhāvitā dhvajāḥ bahuvidha ākārāḥ mīna vyāla ādi citritāḥ vitresuḥ amarāḥ sarve śaktīnām bhaṅga śaṅkayā te karaṅka mukhāḥ pañca senāpatayaḥ uddhatāḥ sarpiṇīm nāma samare māyām cakruḥ mahīyasīm taiḥ samutpatitā duṣṭā sarpiṇī ramaśāṃbarī dhūmravarṇā ca dhūmroṣṭhī dhūmravarmapayodharā puras cacāla śaktīn āntrāsayantī manaḥ raṇe kadrūḥ iva aparā duṣṭā bahu sarpa vibhūṣaṇā sarpāṇām udbhava sthānam māyā maya śarīriṇām senāpatīnām nāsīre vellayantī mahī tale vellitam bahudhā cakre ghora ārāva virāviṇī tathā eva māyayā pūrvam te asura idrāḥ vyajījayan karaṅka ādyāḥ durātmānaḥ pañca pañcattva kāmukāḥ atha pravavṛte yuddham śaktīnām amara druhām anyonya vīra bhāṣābhiḥ protsāhita ghana krudhām atyanta saṃkula tayā na vijñāta parasparāḥ śaktayaḥ dānavaḥ ca eva prajahuḥ śastra pāṇayaḥ anyonya śastra saṃghaṭṭa samutthita hutāśane ati niṣṭhura vidhvaṃsi siṃhanāda bhayaṅkare rajaḥ mule rākṣasī tṛpti dāyini śa strī śaraṇi vicchinna daitya kaṇṭha utthita pravṛtte ghora saṃgrāme śaktīnām ca suradviṣām atha sva balam ādāya pañcabhiḥ preritā satī sarpiṇī bahudhā sarpān visasarja śarīrataḥ takṣa karkeṭaka samāḥ vāsuki pramukha tviṣaḥ nānāvidha vapuḥ varṇāḥ nānā dṛṣṭi bhayaṅkarāḥ nānāvidha viṣa jvālā nirdagdha bhuvana trayāḥ dāradam vatsanābham ca kālakūṭam atha aparam saurāṣṭram ca viṣam ghoram brahmaputram atha aparam pratipannam śauklikeyam anyāni api viṣāṇi ca dhūmra varṇāḥ dvi vadanā sarpāḥ ati bhayaṅkarāḥ sarpiṇyāḥ nayana dvandvāḥ dutthitāḥ krodha dīpitāḥ pīta varṇāḥ triphaṇakāḥ daṃṣṭrābhiḥ vikaṭa ānanāḥ sarpiṇyāḥ karṇa kuharāt utthitāḥ sarpa koṭayaḥ āsya ādāḥ nīla vapuṣaḥ sarpiṇyāḥ phaṇinaḥ abhavan anyaiḥ ca bala varṇāḥ ca catur vaktrāḥ catuṣpadāḥ nāsikā vivarāt tasyāḥ udgatāḥ ugra rociṣaḥ laṃbamāna mahā carma āvṛtta sthūla payodharāt nābhikuṇḍāt ca bahavaḥ rakta varṇāḥ bhayānakāḥ halāhalam vahantaḥ ca protthitāḥ pannaga adhipāḥ vidaśantaḥ śakti senām dahantaḥ viṣa vahnibhiḥ badhnantaḥ bhoga pāśaiḥ ca nighnantaḥ phaṇa maṇḍalaiḥ atyantam ākulām cakruḥ lalitā īśī camūm amī khaṇḍyamānāḥ api muhur śaktīnām śastra koṭibhiḥ naśyanti bahavaḥ sarpāḥ jāyante ca apare punar mūla bhūtā yatas duṣṭā sarpiṇī na vinaśyati atas tad kṛta sarpāṇām nāśe sarpa antara udbhavaḥ tatas ca śakti sainyānām śarīrāṇi viṣa analaiḥ kiṅkartavya vimūḍheṣu śakti cakreṣu bhogibhiḥ parākramam bahuvidham cakruḥ te pañca dānavāḥ cakreṇa tīkṣṇa dhāreṇa śakti senām amardayat vajradanta abhidhaḥ ca anyaḥ bhaṇḍa daitya camūpatiḥ vajra bāṇa abhighātena ha uṣṭrataḥ hi raṇam vyadhāt vajradanta abhidhānaḥ anyaḥ camūnām adhipaḥ balī gṛdhra yugma ratha ārūḍhaḥ prajahāra śilīmukhaiḥ taiḥ senāpatibhiḥ duṣṭaiḥ protsāhitam atha āhave śatam akṣauhiṇīnām ca nipapāta eka helayā sarpiṇī ca durācārā bahu māyā parigrahā kṣaṇekṣaṇe koṭi saṃkhyān visasarja phaṇa adharān nakulī garuḍa ārūḍhā sā papāta raṇa ajire samasta vāc maya ākārā dantaiḥ vajra mayaiḥ yutā tayā adhiṣṭhita tuṅga aṃsaḥ pakṣa vikṣipta bhūdharaḥ sarpiṇī māyayā jātān sarpān dṛṣṭvā bhayānakān atha śrī nakulī devyāḥ dvātriṃśat danta koṭayaḥ dvātriṃśat koṭayaḥ jātāḥ nakulāḥ kanaka prabhāḥ itas tatas khaṇḍayantaḥ sarpiṇī sarpa maṇḍalam nija daṃṣṭrā vimardena nāśayantaḥ ca tat viṣam utkarṇāḥ krodha samparkāt hūnita aśeṣa lomakāḥ utphullāḥ nakulāḥ vyātta vadanāḥ vyadaśan ahīn tīkṣṇa danta nipātena khaṇḍayāmāsa vigraham bhogi bhoga sṛtaiḥ raktaiḥ sṛkkiṇī śoṇa tām gate nakulaiḥ daśyamānānām atyanta caṭulam vapuḥ muhur kuṇḍalitaiḥ bhogaiḥ pannagānām vyaceṣṭata nakula āvali daṣṭānām naṣṭa asūnām phaṇābhṛtām phaṇa ābhara samutkīrṇāḥ maṇayaḥ vyarucan raṇe nakula āghāta saṃśīrṇa phaṇā cakraiḥ vinirgataiḥ phaṇayaḥ tad mahā droha vahvi jvālāḥ iva ābabhuḥ evaṃprakārataḥ babhru maṇḍalaiḥ avakhaṇḍite māyā maye sarpa jāle sarpiṇī kopam ādadhe tayā saha mahat yuddham kṛtvā sā nakula īśvarī gāruḍa astram ati krūram samādhatta śilīmukhe tat gāruḍa astram uddāma jvālā dīpita diṅmukham praviśya sarpiṇī deham sarpa māyām vyaśoṣayat māyā śaktoḥ vināśena sarpiṇī vilayam gatā krodham ca tad vināśena prāptāḥ pañca camū varāḥ sā sarpiṇī kathā śeṣam nītā nakula vīryataḥ atas sva bala nāśena bhṛśam kruddhāḥ camū carāḥ ekā eva sā tārkṣyarathā pañcabhiḥ pṛtanā īśvarī paṭṭiśaiḥ musalaiḥ ca eva bhindipālaiḥ sahasraśas tatas hāhā rutam ghoram kurvāṇāḥ daitya kiṅkarāḥ udagra daṃśa nakulaiḥ nakulaiḥ ākulīkṛtāḥ utpatya gaganāt kecid ghora cītkāra kāriṇaḥ deśantaḥ tad dviṣām sainya sa kulāḥ prajvala krudhaḥ karṇeṣu daṣṭvā nāsāyām anye daṣṭāḥ śiraḥ taṭe pṛṣṭhatas pyadaśan kecid ā gatya vyākṛta kriyāḥ vikalāḥ chinna varmāṇaḥ bhaya visrasta śastrikāḥ kecid praviśya nakulāḥ vyāttāni āsyāni vairiṇām bhogi bhogāni vā ākṛṣya vyadaśan rasanā talam anye karṇeṣu nakulāḥ prāviśan deva vairiṇām sūkṣma rūpāḥ viśantisma nānā randhrāṇi babhravaḥ nija sainyāni dīnāni karaṅkaḥ kopam āsthitaḥ anye api ca camū nāthāḥ laghu hastāḥ mahā balāḥ pratibabhru śara stomān vavṛṣuḥ vāridāḥ iva daitya sainya pati prauḍha kodaḍa utthāḥ śilīmukhāḥ babhrūṇām danta koṭīṣu kaṭhora ghaṭṭanam vyadhuḥ camūpati śakhi ūhaiḥ āhatebhyaḥ paraḥśataiḥ babhrūṇām vajra datebhyaḥ niścakrāma hutāśanaḥ pañca api te camū nātha visṛṣṭaiḥ eka helayā itas tatas camū nātha vikṣipta śara koṭibhiḥ viśīrṇa gātrāḥ nakulāḥ nakulīm paryavārayan atha sā nakulī vāṇī vāṅmayasya eka nāyikā nakulānām parāvṛttyā mahāntam roṣam āśritā akṣīṇanakulam nāma mahā astram sarvatomukham vahni jvālā parīta agram saṃdadhe śārṅgadhanvani tad astrataḥ viniṣṭhyūtāḥ nakulāḥ koṭi saṃkhyākāḥ vajra aṅgāḥ vajra lomānaḥ vajra daṃṣṭrāḥ mahā javā vajra sārāḥ ca nibiḍā vajra jāla bhayaṅkarā vajra ākāraiḥ naśaiḥ tūrṇa dārayantaḥ mahī talam vajra ratna prakāśena locanena api śobhitāḥ vajra saṃpāta sadṛśāḥ nāsā cītkāra kāriṇaḥ mardayanti sura arāti sainyam daśana koṭibhiḥ vinaṣṭāḥ pratyavayavam vineśuḥ dānava adhamāḥ evam vajra mayaiḥ babhuḥ maṇḍalaiḥ śaṇḍite bale śatākṣauhiṇike saṃkhye te sva mātra avaśeṣitāḥ ati trāsena roṣeṇa gṛhītāḥ ca camū varāḥ saṃgrāmam adhikam tenuḥ samākṛṣṭa śarāsanāḥ taiḥ samam bahudhā yuddham tanvānā nakula īśvarī paṭṭiśena karaṅkasya ciccheda kaṭhinam śiraḥ kāka vāśita sukhyānām caturṇām api vairiṇām utpatya utpatya tārkṣyeṇa vyalunāt asinā śiraḥ tādṛśam lāghavam dṛṣṭvā nakulyā śyāmala aṃbikā bahu mene mahā sattvām duṣṭa asura vināśinīm nija aṅga deva tattvam ca tasyai śyāmā aṃbikā dadau lokottare guṇe dṛṣṭe kasya na prīti saṃbhavaḥ hata śiṣṭāḥ bhīta bhītāḥ nakulī śaraṇam gatāḥ sā api tān vīkṣya kṛpayā mā bhaiṣṭa iti vihasya ca bhavat rājñe raṇa udantam aśeṣam ca nibodhata tayā evam preṣitāḥ śīghram tat ālokya raṇa kṣitim muditāḥ te punar bhītyā śūnya kāyām palāyitāḥ tat udantam tatas śrutvā bhaṇḍaḥ caṇḍaḥ ruṣā abhavat iti brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge lalitopākhyāne karaṅkādipañcasenāpativadhaḥ nāma trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ hateṣu teṣu roṣa andhaḥ niśvasan śūnyakeśvaraḥ proce yuyutsā vyākula āśayaḥ karaṅka ādyaḥ camū nāthāḥ kandalat bhuja vikramāḥ sarpiṇī māyayā sarva gīrvāṇa mada bhañjanāḥ pāpīyasyā tayā gūḍha māyayā vinipātitāḥ balāhaka prabhṛtayaḥ sapta ye sainika adhipāḥ tri śatam ca akṣauhiṇīnām prasthāpaya saha eva taiḥ te mardayitvā lalitā sainyam māyā parāyaṇāḥ kīkasa garbha saṃjātāḥ te pracaṇḍa parākramāḥ balāhaka mukhāḥ sapta bhrātaraḥ jayinaḥ sadā teṣām avaśyam vijayaḥ bhaviṣyati raṇa aṅgaṇe iti bhaṇḍāsureṇa uktaḥ kuṭilākṣaḥ samāhvayat balāhaka mukhān sapta senā nāthān mada utkaṭān balāhakaḥ prathamatas tasmāt sūcīmukhaḥ aparaḥ anyaḥ phāla mukhaḥ ca eva vikarṇaḥ vikaṭa ānanaḥ karālāyuḥ karaṭakaḥ sapta ete vīrya śālinaḥ bhaṇḍāsuram namaskṛtya yuddha kautūhala ulvaṇāḥ kīkasā sūnavaḥ sarve bhrātaraḥ anyonyam āvṛtāḥ triśāta akṣauhiṇī senā senān yaḥ anvagaman tadā ghora saṃgrāmiṇī pādā ghātaiḥ mardita bhū talā pibanti dhūlikā jālaiḥ aśeṣān api sāgarān bherī niḥ sāṇa taṃpoṭṭa paṇava ānaka nisvanaiḥ nabhaḥ guṇa mayam viśvam ādadhānāḥ pade pade tri śata akṣauhiṇī senām tām gṛhītvā madet hatāḥ dhṛta roṣa aruṇāḥ sūrya maṇḍalaḥ ddīpta kaṅkaṭāḥ uddīpta śastra bharaṇāḥ celuḥ dīpta ūrdhva keśinaḥ sapta lokān pramathitum proṣitāḥ pūrvam uddhatāḥ bhaṇḍāsureṇa mahatā jagat vijaya kāriṇā sapta loka vimardena tena dṛṣṭvā mahā balāḥ proṣitāḥ lalitā sainyam jetu kāmena muhur kilakilā rābaiḥ ghoṣayantaḥ diśaḥ daśa sainyam ca lalitā devyāḥ sannaddham śāstra bhīṣaṇam pāśinyaḥ musalinyaḥ ca cakriṇyaḥ ca aparāḥ mune mudgariṇyaḥ paṭṭiśinyaḥ kodaṇḍinyaḥ tathā aparāḥ anekāḥ śaktayaḥ tīvrāḥ lalitā sainya saṃgatāḥ āyāta āyāta he duṣṭāḥ pāpinyaḥ vanitā adhamāḥ māyā parigrahaiḥ dūram mohayantyaḥ jaḍa āśayān śvasat bhujaga saṃkāśaiḥ bāṇaiḥ a tyanta bhīṣaṇaiḥ iti śaktīḥ bhartsayantaḥ dānavāḥ cakruḥ āhavam kācid ciccheda daitya indram kaṇṭhe paṭṭiśa pātanāt tatra lagnāḥ bahutarāḥ gṛdhrāḥ maṇḍala tām gatāḥ kācid śaktiḥ murārātim mukta śakti āyudham raṇe ekā tu gajam ārūḍhā kasyacid daitya durmateḥ uraḥsthale sva kariṇā vapra āghātam aśikṣayat kācid pratibhaṭa ārūḍham dantinam kuṃbha sīmani dhanuḥ daṇḍam dvidhā kṛtvā sva bhruvoḥ pratimām tanet śaktiḥ anyā śaraiḥ śātaiḥ śātayitvā virodhinaḥ kṛpāṇa padmā romālyām svakīyāyām mudam vyadhāt kācid mudgara pātena cūrṇayitvā virodhinaḥ abhyantaram śakti senā daityānām praviveśa ha praviveśa ca daityānām senā śakti bala antaram nīra kṣīra vat atyanta āśleṣam śakti suradviṣām saṃkula ākāra tām prāptaḥ yuddha kāle abhavat tadā śaktīnām khaḍga pātena lūna śuṇḍārada dvayāḥ daityānām kariṇaḥ mattāḥ mahā kroḍāḥ iva abhavan evam pravṛtte samare vīrāṇām ca bhayaṅkare aśakye smartum api antam kātara tvavatām nṛṇām bhīṣaṇānām bhīṣaṇe ca śastra vyāpāra durgame balāhakaḥ mahāgṛdhram vajra tīkṣṇa mukha ādikam kāla daṇḍa upamam jaṅghā kāṇḍe caṇḍa parākramam saṃhāragupta nāmānam pūrvam agre samutthitam dhūma vat dhūsara ākāram pakṣa kṣepa bhayaṅkaram pakṣau vitatya krośa ardham sa sthitaḥ bhīma niḥsvanaiḥ aṅgāra kuṇḍa vat cañcum vidārya abhakṣayat camūm saṃhāra guptam sa mahā gṛdhraḥ krūra vilocanaḥ balāhakam uvāha uccais ākṛṣṭa dhanuṣam raṇe balāhakaḥ vapuḥ dhunvan gṛdhra pṛṣṭha kṛta sthitiḥ sapakṣa kūṭa śaila sthaḥ balāhakaḥ iva abhavat sūcīmukhaḥ ca daitya indraḥ sūcī niṣṭhura pakṣatim kāka vāhanam āruhya kaṭhinam samaram vyadhāt mattaḥ parvata śṛṅga ābhaḥ cañcū daṇḍam samudvahan kāla daṇḍa pramāṇena jaṅghā kāṇḍena bhīṣaṇaḥ puṣkala āvartaka samā jaṃbāla sadṛśa dyatiḥ krośa mātra āyatau pakṣau ubhau api samudvahan sūcīmukha adhiṣṭhitaḥ asau karaṭaḥ kaṭu vāsitaḥ mardayan cañcu ghātena śaktīnām maṇḍalam mahat atho phalamukhaḥ phālam gṛhītvā nijam āyudham vikarṇa ākhyaḥ ca daitya indraḥ camū bhartā mahā balaḥ bheruṇḍa patana ārūḍhaḥ pracaṇḍa yuddham ātanot vikaṭa ānana nāmānam vilasat paṭṭiśa āyudham uvāha samare caṇḍaḥ kukkuṭaḥ ati bhayaṅkaraḥ garjan kaṇṭha stha romāṇi harṣayan jvalat īkṣaṇaḥ paśyan puras śakti sainyam cacāla caraṇa āyudhaḥ karālākṣaḥ ca bhūbhartā ṣaṣṭhaḥ atyanta gariṣṭha daḥ vajra niṣṭhura ghoṣaḥ ca prācalat preta vāhanaḥ śmaśāna mantra śūreṇa tena saṃsādhitaḥ purā pretaḥ bhūta samāviṣṭaḥ tam uvāha raṇa ajire avāk mukhaḥ dīrgha bāhuḥ prasārita pada dvayaḥ protaḥ vāhana tām prāptaḥ karāla akṣam atha avahat anyaḥ karaṭakaḥ nāma daitya senā śikhāmaṇiḥ sardayāmāsa śaktīnām sainyam vetālavāhanaḥ yojana āyata mūrtiḥ san vetālaḥ krūra locanaḥ śmaśāna bhūmau vetālaḥ mantreṇa anena sādhitaḥ mardayāmāsa pṛtanām śaktīnām tena deśitaḥ bahudhā ayudhyata tadā śaktibhiḥ saha dānavaḥ evam ete khala ātmānaḥ sapta sapta arṇava upamāḥ śaktīnām sainikam tatra vyākulīcakruḥ uddhatāḥ tena dattaḥ varaḥ teṣām tapaḥ tuṣṭena bhāsvatā kaikaseyāḥ mahābhāgāḥ bhavatām tapasā adhunā parituṣṭaḥ asmi bhadram vaḥ bhavantaḥ vṛṇatām varam iti ukte dinanāthena kaikaseyāḥ tapaḥ kṛśāḥ prārthayāmāsuḥ atyartham durdāntam varam īdṛśam raṇeṣu sannidhātavyam asmākam netra kukṣiṣu tvayā yadā sannihitam tapana asmākam akṣiṣu tadā akṣi viṣayaḥ sarvaḥ niśceṣṭaḥ bhavatāt prabho tvad sānnidhya samiddhena netreṇa asmākam īkṣitāḥ tatas stabdheṣu śastreṣu vīkṣaṇāt eva naḥ prabho niśceṣṭāḥ ripavaḥ asmābhiḥ hantavyāḥ sukara tvataḥ iti pūrvam varaḥ prāptaḥ kaikaseyauḥ divākarāt atha sūrya samāviṣṭa netraiḥ teḥ tu nirīkṣitāḥ śaktayaḥ stabdha śastra oghāḥ viphala utsāḥ hatām gatāḥ viṣṭaṃbhita astra śastrāṇām śaktīnām na udyamaḥ abhavat abhibhūtāḥ sa niśvāsam śaktayaḥ joṣam āsata atha te vāsaram prāpya nānā praharaṇa udyatāḥ vyamardayan śakti sainyam daityāḥ sva svāmi deśitāḥ śaktayaḥ tāḥ tu sainyena nirvyāpārāḥ nirāyudhāḥ akṣubhyanta śaraiḥ teṣām vajra kaṅkaṭa bhodibhiḥ śaktayaḥ daitya śastra odhaiḥ viddha gātrāḥ sṛtāmṛjaḥ hāhākāram vitanvatyaḥ prapannāḥ laliteśvarīm cukruśuḥ śaktayaḥ sarvāḥ taiḥ staṃbhita nija āyudhāḥ atha devī ājñayā daṇḍanāthā pratyaṅga rakṣiṇī mahāmāyā samāruhya śaktīnām abhayam vyadhāt tamāla śyāmala ākārā śyāma kañcuka dhāriṇī śyāma chāye tamas lipte śyāma yukta turaṅgame vāsantī mohana abhikhyam dhanuḥ ādāya sa svanam siṃhanādam vinadya iṣūn avarṣat sarpa sannibhān kṛṣṇa rūpa bhujaṅga bhān adhas musala saṃnibhān mohana astra viniṣṭhyūtān bāṇān daityāḥ na sehire itas tatas mardyamānāḥ mahā māyā śilīmukhaiḥ prakopam paramam prāptāḥ balāhaka mukhāḥ khalāḥ atho tiraskaraṇī aṃbā daṇḍanāthā nideśataḥ andha abhidham mahā astram sā mumoca dviṣatām gaṇe balāhaka ādyāḥ te sapta dinanātha vara uddhatāḥ andha astreṇa nijam netram dadhire chāditam yathā udgatena andha bāṇena cakṣuḥ teṣām vyadhīyata andhīkṛtāḥ ca te sapta na tu praikṣanta kiñcana tad vīkṣaṇasya virahāt śastra stambhaḥ kṣayam gataḥ punar sa siṃhanādam tāḥ prodyata āyudha pāṇayaḥ cakruḥ samara sannāham daityānām prajighāṃsayā tiraskaraṇikām devīm agre kṛtvā mahā balām sat upāya prasaṅgena bhṛśam tuṣṭāḥ raṇam vyadhuḥ sādhu sādhu mahābhāge tiraskaraṇikā aṃbike sthāne kṛta tiraskārāḥ dvipām eṣām durātmanām tvam hi durjana netrāṇām tiraskāra mahā oṣadhī tvayā baddha dṛśā anena daitya cakreṇa bhūyate asmādṛśām ajayyeṣu yadā eṣu vyasanam kṛtam tat tvayā eva durācārān etān sapta mahā asurān nihatān lalitā śrutvā santoṣam param āpsyati evam tvayā viracite daṇḍinī prīti māpsyati mantriṇī api mahābhāgāyāḥ eva parām mudam tasmāt tvam eva sapta etān nigṛhaṇa raṇa ajire eṣām sainyam tu nikhilam nāśayāmaḥ udāyudhāḥ tām āyāntīm samāvekṣya te sapta atha sura adhamāḥ praviṣṭam api sāvitram na aśakam tad nirodhane vara dāna astra roṣa andham mahā bala parākramam astreṇa ca ruṣā ca andham balāhaka mahā asuram ākṛṣya keśeṣu asinā cakarta antardhi devatā tasya vāhana gṛdhrasya lunānā patriṇā śiraḥ sūcīmukhasya abhimukham tiraskaraṇikā vrajat tasya paṭṭiśa pātena vilūya kaṭhinam śiraḥ anyeṣām api pañcānām pañcatvam akarot śanais taiḥ sapta daitya muṇḍaiḥ ca grathita anyonya keśakaiḥ hāra dāma gale kṛtvā nanāda antardhi devatā hatvā tad rakta salilaiḥ bahvīḥ prāvāhayat nadīḥ tatra āścaryam abhūt bhūri māhāmāyā aṃbikā kṛtam balāhaka ādi senā nyām dṛṣṭi rodhana vaibhavāt hata śiṣṭāḥ katipayāḥ bahu vitrāsa saṅkulāḥ śaraṇam jagmuḥ ati ārttāḥ krandantam śūnyakeśvaram daṇḍinīm ca mahāmāyām praśaṃsanti muhur muhur prasādam aparam cakṣuḥ tasyāḥ ādāyapipriyuḥ sādhu sādhu iti tatrasthāḥ śaktayaḥ kampa maulayaḥ tiraskaraṇikām devīm aślāghanta pade pade iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalita upākhyāne balāhakādisaptasenāpativadhaḥ nāma caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatas śrutvā vadham teṣām tapaḥ balavatām api nyaśvasat kṛṣṇa sarpa indraḥ iva bhaṇḍaḥ mahā asuraḥ bhaṇḍaḥ pracaṇḍa śaiṇḍīryaḥ kāṅkṣamāṇaḥ raṇe jayam yuvarājaḥ api sa krodhaḥ viṣaṅgeṇa yavīyasā bhaṇḍāsuram namaskṛtya mantra sthānam upāgamat atyāptaiḥ mantribhiḥ yuktaḥ kuṭila akṣa puraḥsaraiḥ lalitā vijaye mantram cakāra kvathita āśyaḥ bhaṇḍaḥ uvāca aho bata kula bhraṃśaḥ samāyātaḥ suradviṣām upekṣām adhunā kartum pravṛttaḥ balavān vidhiḥ tādṛśānām iha asmākam āgataḥ ayam viparyayaḥ dīrgha āyuṣam anāyuṣkam durdhātā bhavitavya tā kva sattvam asmad bāhunām kva iyam durllalitā vadhūḥ akāṇḍaḥ eva vidhinā kṛtaḥ ayam niṣṭhuraḥ vidhiḥ durghaṭa śauryayā adhi saṃgrāma bhū cakre senānyaḥ vinipātitāḥ evam uddāma darpa āḍhyā vanitā kā api māyinī imam prasaṃgam vaktum ca jihvā jihvā iti māmakī mayā cāra mukhāt jñātā tasyāḥ vṛttiḥ mahā balā sarveṣām api sainyānām paścāt eva avatiṣṭhate asmin eva hi avasare pārṣṇigrāhaḥ vidhīyatām pārṣṇigraham imam kartum viṣaṅgaḥ caturaḥ bhavet tena prauḍha mada unmatāḥ bahu saṃgrāma durmadāḥ daśa pañca ca senānyaḥ saha yāntu yuyutsayā pṛṣṭhatas parivārāḥ tu na tathā saṃti te punar atas tvam bahu sannāham āvidhāya mada utkaṭaḥ viṣaṅga gupta rūpeṇa pārṣṇigrāham samācara alpīyasī tvayā sārddham senā gacchatu vikramāt sajjāḥ ca lantu senānyaḥ dikpāla vijaya uddhatāḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ ca senānām daśa pañca calantu te tvam gupta veṣaḥ tām duṣṭām sannipatya dṛḍham jahi sā eva niḥśeṣa śaktīnām mūla bhūtā mahīyasī tasyāḥ sa mūla nāśena śakti vṛndam vinaśyati sarveṣām eva paścāt yaḥ rathaḥ calati bhāsuraḥ vahat muhar vījyamānam cāmarāṇām catuṣṭayam uttaṅga ketu saṃghāta likhita aṃbuda maṇḍalaḥ tasmin rathe samāyāti sā dṛṣṭā hariṇa īkṣaṇā nibṛtam saṃnipatya tvam cihnena anena lakṣitām tām vijitya durācārām keśa iṣvā kṛṣya mardaya puratas calite sainye sattva śālini sā vadhūḥ bhavat sahāya bhūtāyām senā indrāṇām iha abhidhā thuklasaḥ puṇḍraketuḥ ca caṇḍabāhuḥ ca kukkuraḥ jaṃbukākṣaḥ jaṃbhanaḥ ca tīkṣṇaśṛṅgaḥ trikaṇṭakaḥ candraguptaḥ ca pañca ete daśa ca uktāḥ camū varāḥ ekaika akṣauhiṇī yuktāḥ pratyekam bhavatā saha āgamiṣyanti senānyaḥ damana ādyāḥ mahā balāḥ tathā gupta samācāraḥ pārṣṇigrāham samācara viṣaṅgam preṣayāmāsa rakṣitam sainyapālakaiḥ atha śrī lalitā devyāḥ pārṣṇigrāha kṛta udyame andhakāraḥ samabhavat tasya bāhya cikīrṣayā nīlakaṇṭha nibha chāyam nibiḍam paprathe tamaḥ kuñjeṣu piṇḍitam iva pradhāvat iva saṃdhiṣu ujjihānam iva kṣoṇī vivarebhyaḥ sahasraśas kvacid dīpa prabhā jāle kṛta kātara ceṣṭitam datta avalaṃbanam iva strīṇām karṇa utpala tviṣi kṛta priya āśleṣam iva sphurantīṣu asi yaṣṭiṣu gupta praviṣṭam iva ca śyāmāsu vana paṅktiṣu krameṇa bahulībhūtam prasasāra mahattamaḥ triyāmā vāma nayanā nīla kañcuka rociṣā timireṇa āvṛtam viśvam na kiñcid pratyapadyata asurāṇām praduṣṭānām rātriḥ eva bala āvahā teṣām māyā vilāsaḥ ayam tasyām eva hi vardhate atha pracalitam sainyam viṣaṅgeṇa mahā ojasā dhauta khaḍga latā chāyā vardhiṣṇu timira chaṭam damana ādyāḥ ca senānyaḥ śmāma kaṅkaṭa dhāriṇaḥ śyāma uṣṇīṣa dharāḥ śyāma varṇa sarva paricchadāḥ eka tvam iva saṃprāptāḥ timireṇa ati bhūyasā viṣaṅgam anusaṃceluḥ kṛta agraja namaskṛtim kūṭena yuddha kṛtyena vijigīṣuḥ maheśvarīm meghaḍaṃbarakam nāma dadhe vakṣasi kaṅkaṭam yathā tasya niśā yuddha anurūpaḥ veṣa saṃgrahaḥ tathā kṛtavatī senā śyāmalam kañcuka ādikam paṇava ānaka bherīṇām na ca ghoṣa vijṛṃbhaṇam gupta ācārāḥ pracalitāḥ timireṇa samāvṛtāḥ paraiḥ adṛśya gatayaḥ viṣkośīkṛta riṣṭayaḥ paścima abhimukham yānti lalitāyāḥ patākinīm āvṛta uttara mārgeṇa pūrva bhāgam aśiśriyan sa avadhānāḥ pracalitāḥ pārṣṇigrāhāya dānavāḥ bhūyas purasya digbhāgam gatvā manda parākramāḥ āgatya nibhṛtam pṛṣṭhe kavaca channa vigrahāḥ apaśyan ati dīptābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ parivāritam sahasra āditya saṃkāśām paścima abhimukhīm sthitām kāma īśvarā ādi nityābhiḥ sva samāna samṛddhibhiḥ tām tathā bhūta vṛttāntām a tādṛśa raṇa udyamām purogatam mahat sainyam vīkṣamāṇa sa kautukam manvānaḥ ca hi tām eva viṣaṅgaḥ su durāśayaḥ pṛṣṭhavaṃśe ratha indrasya ghaṭṭayāmāsa sainikaiḥ tatra aṇi mā ādi śaktīnām parivāra varūthinī mahā kalakalam cakruḥ aṇima ādyāḥ paraḥśatam paṭṭiśaiḥ drughaṇaiḥ ca eva bhindipālaiḥ bhuśuṇḍibhiḥ kaṭhora vajra nirdhāta niṣṭhuraiḥ śakti maṇḍalaiḥ ākasmikaraṇa utsāha viparyāviṣṭa vigraham akāṇḍa kṣubhitam ca āsīt ratha stham śakti maṇḍalam vipāṭaiḥ pāṭayāmāsuḥ adṛśyaiḥ andhakāriṇaḥ adṛśyamāna śastrāṇām adṛśya nija varmaṇām timira channa rūpāṇām dānavānām śilīmukhaiḥ śaktīnām maṇḍalam tene krandanam lalitām prati karṇa ākarṇikayā ākarṇya lalitā kopam ādadhe etasmin antare bhaṇḍaḥ caṇḍa durmatri paṇḍitaḥ daśa akṣauhiṇikā yuktam kuṭila akṣam mahā ojasam lalitā sainya nāśāya yuddhāya prajighāya saḥ yathā paścāt kalakalam śrutvā agrevartinī camūḥ na āgacchati tathā cakre kuṭilākṣaḥ mahā raṇam atyanta tumulam ca āsīt śaktīnām sainike mahat naktasattvāḥ ca daitya indrāḥ timireṇa samāvṛtāḥ itas tatas śithila tām kaṇṭake ninyuḥ uddhatāḥ niṣaṅgeṇa durāśena dhamana ādyaiḥ camū varaiḥ camūbhiḥ ca praṇahitāḥ nyapatan śatru koṭayaḥ tābhiḥ daitya astra mālābhiḥ cakrarāja rathaḥ vṛtaḥ baka āvalī nibiḍataḥ śailarājaḥ iva ābabhau ākrānta parvaṇā adhastāt viṣaṅgeṇa durātmanā muktaḥ ekaḥ śaraḥ devyāḥ tālavṛntam acūrṇayat atha tena avyāhitena saṃbhrānte śakti maṇḍale kāmeśvarī mukhāḥ nityāḥ mahāntam krodham āyayuḥ īṣat bhṛkuṭi saṃsaktam śrī devyāḥ vadana aṃbujam nityā kāla svarūpiṇyaḥ pratyekam tithi vigrahāḥ praṇipatya ca tām devīm mahā rājñīm mahodayām ūcuḥ vācam akāṇḍa utthām yuddha kautuka gadgadām devadevī mahā rājñī tava agre brekṣitām camūm daṇḍinī mantranātha ādi mahā śakti ābha pālitām kātarāḥ duṣṭāḥ māyā chadma parāyaṇāḥ pārṣṇigrāheṇa yuddhena bādhante ratha puṅgavam tasmāt timira saṃchanna mūrtīnām vibudha druhām śamayāmaḥ vayam darpam kṣaṇa mātram vilokaya yā vahni vāsinī nityā yā jvālā mālinī parā tābhyām pradīpite yuddhe draṣṭum śaktāḥ suradviṣaḥ praśamayya mahā darpam pārṣṇigrāha pravartinām sahasā eva āgamiṣyāmaḥ sevitum śrī pada aṃbujam ājñām dehi mahā rājñi mardana artham durātmanām atha kāmeśvarī nityā praṇamya laliteśvarīm tayā saṃpreṣitā tābhiḥ kuṇḍalīkṛta kārmukā sā hantum tān durācārān kūṭa yuddha kṛtakṣaṇān bāla aruṇam iva krodha aruṇam vaktram vitanvatī re re tiṣṭhata pāpiṣṭhāḥ māyā niṣṭhāḥ chinadmi vaḥ andhakāram anuprāpya kūṭa yuddha parāyaṇāḥ iti tān bhartsayantī sā tūṇīra utkhāta sāyakāt sajja kārmuka hastāḥ ca bhaga mālā puraḥsarāḥ anyāḥ ca caritāḥ nityāḥ kṛta parva avarohaṇāḥ jvālā mālini nityā ca yā nityā vahni vāsinī atha te duṣṭa danujāḥ pradīpte yuddha maṇḍale prakāśa vapuṣaḥ tatra mara antam krodham āyayuḥ kāmeśvarī ādikāḥ nityāḥ tāḥ pañcadaśa sa āyudhāḥ sa siṃhanādāḥ tān daityān amṛdnan eva helayā tāḥ ca nitya avalat kvāṇa kaṅkaṇaiḥ yudhi pāṇibhiḥ ākṛṣya prāma kodaṇḍāḥ tenire yuddham uddhatam nityānām niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ ca saṃhṛtāḥ jaghāna damanam duṣṭam kāmeśī prathamam śaraiḥ dīrghajihvam camū nātham bhaga mālā vyadārat kaklasam vahni vāsā ca nijaghāna śaraiḥ śataiḥ mahā vajra īśvarī bāṇaiḥ abhinat kekivāhanam puklasam śivadūtī ca prāhiṇot yama sādanam puṇḍraketum bhuja uddaṇḍam tvaritā samadārayat kulasundarikā nityā caṇḍabāhum ca kukkuram jaṃbuka akṣam jṛṃbhaṇam ca vyatanvātām raṇe balim sarva maṅgalikā nityā tīkṣṇa śṛṅgam akhaṇḍayat jvālā mālinikā nityā jaghāna ugram tri karṇakam candraguptam ca duḥśīlam citram citrā vyadārat senā nātheṣu sarveṣu nihateṣu durātmasu viṣaṅgaḥ paramaḥ kuddhaḥ cacāla puratas balī atha yāma avaśeṣāyām yāminyām ghaṭikā dvayam nityābhiḥ saha saṃgrāmam vidhāya sa durāśayaḥ kāmeśvarī kara ākṛṣṭa cāpa utthauḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhinna varmā dṛḍhataram viṣaṅgaḥ vihvala āśayaḥ hata avaśiṣṭaiḥ yodhaiḥ ca sārdham eva palāyitaḥ tābhiḥ na nihataḥ duṣṭaḥ yasmāt vadhyaḥ sa dānavaḥ daṇḍanāthā śareṇa eva kāla daṇḍa sama tviṣā tasmin palāyite duṣṭe viṣaṅge sā vibhātā ca rajanī prasannāḥ ca abhavan diśaḥ iti tāḥ samarāt nityāḥ tasmin kāle vyaraṃsiṣuḥ nityāḥ śrī lalitām devīm praṇipetuḥ jaya uddhatāḥ nityānām rūpa jālam ca śastra kṣatam alokayat śrutvā udantam mahā rājñī kṛpā apāṅgena sā aikṣata tad ālokana mātreṇa vraṇaḥ nirvraṇa tām agāt nityānām vikramaiḥ ca api lalitā prītim āsadat iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne viṣaṅgapalāyanam nāma pañcaviṃśaḥ adhyāya daśa akṣauhiṇikā yuktaḥ kuṭila akṣaḥ api vīryavān daṇḍanāthā śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ raṇe bhagnaḥ palāyitaḥ daśa akṣauhiṇikam sainyam tayā rātrau vināśitam imam vṛttāntam ākarṇya bhaṇḍaḥ kṣobham atha āyayau rātrau kapaṭa saṃgrāmam duṣṭānām nirjara druhām mantriṇī daṇḍanāthā ca śrutvā nirvedam āpatuḥ mahā cakra ratha indrasya na jātam rakṣaṇam balaiḥ etam tu avasaram prāpya rātrau duṣṭaiḥ parākṛtam kaḥ vṛttāntaḥ abhavat tatra svāminyā kim raṇaḥ kṛtaḥ vimraṣṭavyam idam kāryam pravṛttiḥ tatra kīdṛśī mahādevyāḥ ca hṛdaye kaḥ prasaṃgaḥ pravartate iti śaṅkā ākulāḥ tatra daṇḍanāthā purogamāḥ mantriṇīm puratas kṛtvā praceluḥ lalitām prati śakti cakra camū nāthāḥ sarvāḥ tāḥ pūjitāḥ drutam vyatītāyām vibhāvaryām ratha indram paryavārayan avaruhya sva yānābhyām mantriṇī daṇḍa nāyike abhajetām mahā rājñīm mantriṇī daṇḍa nāyike te vyajijñapatām devyāḥ aṣṭāṅga spṛṣṭa bhū tale mahā pramādaḥ samabhūt iti naḥ śrutam aṃbike kūṭa yuddha prakāreṇa daityaiḥ apakṛtam khalaiḥ sa durātmā durācāraḥ prakāśa samārāt trasan daivāt naḥ svāminī gātre duṣṭānām amara druhām śara ādika parāmarśaḥ na jātaḥ tena jīvati eka avalaṃbanam kṛtvā mahā rājñi bhavat padam vayam sarvāḥ hi jīvāmaḥ sādhayāmaḥ samīhitam atas asmābhiḥ prakartavyam śrīmatī aṅgasya rakṣaṇam āpad kāleṣu jetavyāḥ bhaṇḍa ādyāḥ dānava adhamāḥ kūṭa yuddham na kurvanti na viśanti camūm imām tathā mahendra śailasya kāryam dakṣiṇa deśataḥ śibiram bahu vistāram yojanānām śata avadhi vahli prākāra valayam rakṣaṇa artham vidhīyatām asmad senā niveśasya dviṣām darpa śamāya ca yatas dakṣiṇa deśa stham śūnyakam vidviṣām puram dvāre ca bahavaḥ kalpyāḥ parivārāḥ udāyudhāḥ nirgacchatām praviśatām janānām uparodhakāḥ anālasyāḥ anidrāḥ ca vidheyāḥ satata udyatāḥ evam ca sati duṣṭānām kūṭa yuddham cikīrṣitam avelāsu ca saṃdhyāsu madhyarātriṣu ca dviṣām aśakyam eva bhavati prauḍham ākramaṇam haṭhāt no ced durāśayāḥ daityāḥ bahu māyā parigrahāḥ mantriṇyāḥ daṇḍanāthāyāḥ iti śrutvā vacaḥ tadā śuci danta rucā muktā vahantī lalitā bravīt bhavatīnām ayam mantraḥ cāru buddhyā vicāritaḥ ayam kuśala dhī mārgaḥ nītiḥ eṣā sanātanī sva cakrasya puras rakṣām vidhāya dṛḍha sādhanaiḥ para cakra ākramaḥ kāryaḥ jigīṣadbhiḥ mahājanaiḥ iti uktvā mantriṇī daṇḍanāthe sā laliteśvarī jvālā mālinikām nityām āhūya idam uvāca ha vatse tvam vahni rūpā asi jvālā mālā maya ākṛtiḥ tvayā vidhīyatām rakṣā balasya asya mahīyasaḥ triṃśat yojanam unnaddham jvālā ākāra tvam āvraja vahni jvālā tvam āpannā saṃrakṣa sakalam balam iti uktvā mantriṇī daṇḍanāthe sā laliteśvarī sā ca nitya anitya mayī jvalat jvā lāmaya ākṛtiḥ caturdaśī tithi mayī tathā iti praṇanāma tām kuṇḍalīkṛtya jajvāla śāla rūpeṇa sā punar nabhaḥ valaya jaṃbāla jvālā mālā maya ākṛtiḥ babhāse daṇḍanāthāyāḥ mantri nātha camūḥ api anyā sām api śaktīnām mahatīnām mahat balam viśaṅkaṭa udaram sālam praviveśa gata klamā rāja cakra ratha indram tu madhye saṃsthāpya daṇḍinī vāma pakṣe ratham svīyam dakṣiṇe śyāmalā ratham paścādbhāge sampadeśīm purastāḥ ca haya āsanām dvāre niveśayāmāsa viṃśati akṣauhiṇī yutām jvalat daṇḍa āyudha udagrām stambhinīm nāma devatām yā devī daṇḍanāthāyāḥ vighnadevī iti viśrutā evam su rakṣitam kṛtvā śibiram yotriṇī tathā pūṣaṇi udita bhūyiṣṭhe punar yuddham upāśrayat kṛtvā kilakilā rāvam tatas śakti mahā camūḥ agni prākāraka dvārāt nirjagām mahā ravā ittham su rakṣitam śrutvā lalitā śibira udaram bhūyas saṃjvaram āpannaḥ pracaṇḍaḥ bhaṇḍa dānavaḥ viṣaṅgeṇa viśukreṇa asamam ātma sutaiḥ api caturān yuddha kṛtyeṣu samāhūya sa dānavaḥ preṣayāmāsa yuddhāya bhaṇḍaḥ caṇḍa krudhā jvalan triṃśat saṃkhyāḥ ca tad putrāḥ mahā kāyāḥ mahā balāḥ teṣām nāmāni vakṣyāmi samākarṇaya kumbhaja caturbāhuḥ cakorākṣaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu catuḥśirāḥ vajra ghoṣaḥ ca ūrdhva keśaḥ mahā kāyaḥ mahā hanuḥ laḍunaḥ paṭṭasenaḥ ca purājit pūrva mārakaḥ atimāyaḥ bṛhat māyaḥ upamāyaḥ ca vīryavān pituḥ sadṛśa dos vīryāḥ pituḥ sadṛśa vigrahāḥ āgatya bhaṇḍa caraṇau abhyavandata bhaktitaḥ tān udvīkṣya prasannābhyām locanābhyām sa dānavaḥ sa gauravam idam vākyam babhāṣe kula ghātakaḥ bho bho madīyāḥ tanayāḥ bhavatām kaḥ samaḥ bhuvi bhavatām eva satyena jitam viśvam mayā purā śakrasya agneḥ yamasya api nirṛteḥ pāśinaḥ tathā kaceṣu karṣaṇam kopāt kṛtam yuṣmābhiḥ āhave astrāṇi api ca śastrāṇi jānītha nikhilāni api jāgratsu eva hi yuṣmāsu kula bhraṃśaḥ ayam āgataḥ māyāvinī dulalitā kācid strī yuddha durmadā bahubhiḥ sva samānābhiḥ strībhiḥ yuktā hinasti naḥ tat enām samare avaśyam ātma vaśyām vidhāsyatha jīva grāham ca sā grāhyā bhavadbhiḥ jvalat āyudhaiḥ aprameya prakopa andhān vaḥ ekām striyam prati sampreṣaṇam anaucityam tathā api eṣa vidheḥ kramaḥ iti uktvā bhaṇḍa daitya indraḥ tān prahaiṣīt raṇam prati dviśatam ca akṣauhiṇīnām tad sahāya tayā ahinot dviśatī akṣauhiṇī senā mukhyasya tilakāyitā baddha bhrukuṭayaḥ śastra pāṇayaḥ niryayuḥ gṛhāt nirgame bhaṇḍa putrāṇām bhūḥ prakampam alambata utpātāḥ vividhāḥ jātāḥ vitrastam ca abhavat jagat tān kumārān mahāsattvān lāja varṣaiḥ avākiran vithīṣu yānaiḥ calitān paura vṛddha purandhrayaḥ bandinaḥ māgadhāḥ ca eva kumārāṇām stutim vyadhuḥ maṅgala ārārtikam cakruḥ dvāre dvāre pura aṅganāḥ bhidyamānā iva vasudhā kṛṣyamāṇam iva abaram āsīt teṣām viniryāṇe ghūrṇamānaḥ iva arṇavaḥ dviśati akṣauhiṇī senām gṛhītvā śakti sainyāni sarvāṇi bhakṣayāmaḥ kṣaṇāt raṇe teṣām āyudha cakrāṇi cūrṇayāmaḥ śita aiśaraiḥ agni prākāra valayam śamayāmaḥ ca raṃhasā durvidagdhām tām lalitām bandīkurmaḥ ca sarvaram iti anyonyam pravalgantaḥ vīra bhāṣaṇa ghoṣaṇaiḥ āseduḥ agni prākāra samīpam bhaṇḍa sūnavaḥ yauvanena madena andhāḥ bhūyasā ruddha dṛṣṭayaḥ bhrukuṭī kuṭilāḥ cakruḥ siṃhanādam mahāttaram vidīrṇam iva tena āsīt brahmāṇḍa caṇḍima spṛśā utpāta vārida utsṛṣṭa ghora nirghāta raṃhasā etasya ananubhūtasya mahā śabdasya ḍambaraḥ kṣobhayāmāsa śaktīnām śravāṃsi ca manāṃsi ca catur bāhu makhān bhūtvā āgatān yuddha kṛtyāya bālā kautūhalam dadhe kumārī lalitā devyāḥ tasyāḥ nikaṭa vāsinī samasta śakti cakrāṇām pūjya vikrama śālinī lalitā sadṛśa ākārā kumārī kopam ādadhe yā sadā nava varṣā iva sarva vidyā mahā khaniḥ bāla aruṇa tanuḥ śroṇī śoṇa varṇa vapuḥ latā mahā rājñī pāda pīṭhe nityam āhita saṃnidhiḥ tasyāḥ bahis carāḥ prāṇāḥ yā caturtham vilocanam tān āgatān bhaṇḍa sutān saṃhariṣyāmi sa tvaram iti niścitya bāla aṃbā mahā rājñyai vyajijñapat mātarbhaṇḍa mahā daitya sūnavaḥ yoddhum āgatāḥ saphurantau iva me bāhū yuddha kaṇḍūyayā anayā krīḍā mama eṣā hantavyā na bhavatyā nivāraṇaiḥ aham hi vālikā nityam krīḍaneṣu anurāgiṇī kṣaṇam raṇa krīḍayā ca prītim yāsyāmi ca etasā iti vijñāpitā devī pratyuvāca kumārikām vatse tvam ati mṛdu aṅgī nava varṣā nava kramā navīna yuddha śikṣā ca kumārī tvam mama aikikā tvām vinā kṣaṇa mātram me na niśvāsaḥ pravartate daṇḍinī mantriṇī ca eva śaktayaḥ anyāḥ ca koṭiśas iti śrī lalitā devyā niruddhā api kumārikā kaumāra kautuka āviṣṭā punar yuddham ayācata su dṛḍham niścayam dṛṣṭvā tasyāḥ śrī lalitā aṃbikā anujñām kṛtavatī eva gāḍham āśliṣya bāhubhiḥ karṇīratham mahā rājñyā cāpa daṇḍāt samuddhṛtam tasyām raṇe pravṛttāyām sarva parva stha devatāḥ baddhāñjali puṭāḥ nemuḥ pradhṛta asi paraṃparāḥ tābhiḥ praṇamyamānā sā cakrarāja ratha uttamāt tām āyāntīm atho dṛṣṭvā kumārīm kopa pāṭalām mantriṇī daṇḍanāthe ca sa bhaye vācam ūcatuḥ kim bhartṛ dārike yuddhe vyavasāyaḥ kṛtaḥ tvayā akāṇḍe kim mahā rājñyā preṣitā asi raṇam prati tvam mūrtam jīvitam asi śrī devyāḥ bālike yatas nivartasva raṇa utsāhāt praṇāmaḥ te vidhīyate iti tābhyām prārthitā api prācalat dṛḍha niścayā atyantam vismaya āviṣṭe mantriṇī daṇḍa nāyike saha eva tasyāḥ rakṣā artham celatuḥ pārśvayoḥ dvayoḥ atha agnivaraṇa dvārā tābhyām anugatā satī prabhūta senā yuktābhyām nirjagāma kumārikā sa nātha śakti senānām sarvāsām anugṛhṇatī praṇāma añjali jālāni karṇīratha kṛta āsanā bhaṇḍasya tanayān duṣṭān abhyadravat arindamā tasyāḥ prādeśikam sainyam kumāryāḥ na hi vidyate vavarṣa śara jālāni daitya indreṣu kumārikā bhaṇḍāsura kumāraiḥ taiḥ mahā rājñī kumārikā atyanta vismitāḥ daitya kumārāḥ nava varṣiṇīm karmī ratha sthām ālokya kiranti iṃśara maṇḍalam kṣaṇekṣaṇe bālikayā kriyamāṇam mahā raṇam vyajijñapat mahā rājñyai bhramantyaḥ paricārikāḥ mantriṇī daṇḍanāthe ca na tām vijahatuḥ raṇe prekṣaka tva m anuprāpte tṛṣṇīm eva babhūvatuḥ sarveṣām daitya putrāṇām eka rūpā kumārikā pratyeka bhinnā dadṛśe biṃba mālā iva bhāsvataḥ sāyakaiḥ agni cūḍālaiḥ teṣām marmāṇi bhindatī āścaryam bruvataḥ vyomni paśyatām tridivaukasām sādhuvādaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ matriṇī daṇḍanāthayoḥ arcyamānā raṇam cakre laghu hastā kumārikā prakāśayāmāsa balam lalitā duhitā nijam nārāyaṇa astra mokṣeṇa maha rājñī kumārikā dviśati akṣauhiṇī sainyam bhasmasādakarot kṣaṇāt akṣauhiṇīnām kṣayataḥ kṣaṇāt kopam upāgatāḥ ākṛṣṭa guru dhanvānaḥ te apatan eka helayā tatas kalakale jāte śaktīnām ca divaukasām yugapad triṃśataḥ bāṇān asṛjat sā kumārikā hasta lāghavam āśritya muktaiḥ candra ardha sāyakaiḥ triṃśatā triṃśataḥ sāhatam śiraḥ iti bhaṇḍasya putreṣu prāpteṣu yama sādanam atyanta vismaya āviṣṭāḥ vabṛṣuḥ puṣpam abhragāḥ sā ca putrī mahā rājñyāḥ vidhvasta asura mainikā mantriṇī daṇḍanāthābhyām āliṅgyata bhṛśam mudā tasyāḥ parākrama unmeṣaiḥ nṛtyantī ojaya dāyibhiḥ sarvāḥ ca śakti senānyaḥ daṇḍa nāthā puraḥsarāḥ tat āścaryam mahā rājñyai nivedayitum udgatāḥ tābhiḥ nivedyamānāni sā devī lalitā aṃbikā putrī bhuja avadānāni śrutvā prītim samāyayau samastam api tat cakram śaktīnām tad parākramaiḥ a dṛṣṭa pūrvaiḥ deveṣu vismayasya vaśam gatam iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalita upākhyāne bhaṇḍaputravadhaḥ nāma ṣaḍviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha naṣṭeṣu putreṣu śoka anala pariplutaḥ hā putrāḥ hā guṇa udārāḥ hā mad eka parāyaṇāḥ hā mad netra sudhā pūrāḥ hā mad kula vivardhanāḥ hā samasta sura śreṣṭha mada bhañjana tatparāḥ hā samasta sura strīṇām antar mohana manmathāḥ diśata prīti vācam me mama aṅke valgata adhunā kim idānīm imam tātam avamucya sukham gatāḥ yuṣmān vinā na śobhante mama rājyāni putrakāḥ katham evam viniḥśeṣam hatāḥ ayūyam durāśayāḥ apradhṛṣya bhujā sattvān bhavataḥ mad kula aṅkurān katham eka pade duṣṭā vanitā saṃgare avadhīt mama naṣṭāni saukhyāni mama naṣṭāḥ kulastriyaḥ itas param kule kṣīṇe sāhasāni sukhāni ca bhavataḥ sukṛtaiḥ labdhvā mama pūrva januḥ kṛtaiḥ nāśaḥ ayam bhavatām adya jātaḥ naṣṭaḥ tatas asmi aham mūrcchayā lupta hṛdayaḥ niṣpapāta nu pāsanāt viśukraḥ ca viṣaṅgaḥ ca kuṭilākṣaḥ ca saṃsadi bhaṇḍam āśvāsayāmāsuḥ daivasya kuṭila kramaiḥ viśukraḥ uvāca devaki prākṛtaḥ iva prāptaḥ śokasya vaśya tām dharmavān vihitaḥ panthāḥ vīrāṇām eṣa śāśvataḥ etat eva vināśāya śalya vat bādhate manaḥ yat strī samāgatya haṭhāt ni hanti su bhaṭān raṇe bhaṇḍena caṇḍa kālāgni sadṛśaḥ krodhaḥ ādadhe visphārita akṣi yugalaḥ bhṛśam jajvāla tejasā idānīm eva tām duṣṭām khaḍgena anena khaṇḍaśas śakalīkṛtya samare śramam prāpsyāmi bandhubhiḥ tam nirudhya ca saṃbhrāntāḥ sarve dānava puṅgavāḥ na tad arthe tvayā kāryaḥ svāmin saṃbhramaḥ īdṛśaḥ bhavat ājñā lavam prāpya samasta bhuvanam haṭhāt vimarddayitum īśāḥ smaḥ kimu tām mugdha bhāminīm kim cūṣayāmaḥ sapta abdhīn kṣodayāmaḥ atha vā girīn chinadāma surān sarvān bhinadāma tad ālayān pinṣāma haritpālān ājñām dehi mahāmate iti udīrita mā ākarṇya mahā ahaṅkāra garvitam uvāca vacanam kruddhaḥ pratigha aruṇa locanaḥ viśukra bhavatā gatvā mā ayās anta arhita varṣmaṇā jaya vighnam mahā yantram karttavyam kaṭake dviṣām iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā viśukraḥ roṣa rūṣitaḥ paryasta kiraṇa stoma pāṭalī kṛta diṅmukhaḥ anurāgavatī saṃdhyā prayāntam bhānumālinam carama abdheḥ iva payaḥ kaṇāḥ tārāḥ virejire māyā ratham samārūḍhaḥ gūḍha śarvara saṃvṛtaḥ adṛśya vapuḥ āpede lalitā kaṭakam khalaḥ tatra gatvā jvalat jvālam vahni prākāra maṇḍalam paritas vibhraman śālam avakāśam avāpnuvan dakṣiṇam dvāram āsādya nidadhyau kṣaṇam uddhataḥ tatra apaśyat mahāsattvāḥ sa avadhānāḥ dhṛta āyudhāḥ ārūḍha yānāḥ sa naddha varmāṇaḥ dvāra deśataḥ staṃbhinī pramukhāḥ śaktīḥ viśati akṣauhiṇī yutāḥ sarvadā dvāra rakṣā artham nirdiṣṭā daṇḍanāthayā vilokya vismaya āviṣṭaḥ vicārya ca ciram tadā aṣṭa dikṣu aṣṭa śūlena saṃhāra akṣara maulinā alasā kṛpaṇā dīnā nitandrā ca pramīlikā klībā ca nirahaṅkārā ca iti aṣṭau devatāḥ smṛtāḥ devatā aṣṭakam etas ca śūla aṣṭaka puṭa upari pūjām vidhāya mantrasya balibhiḥ chāgala ādibhiḥ tat yantram ca ari kaṭake prākṣipat samare asuraḥ kṣiptam ullaṅghya ca raṇe papāta kaṭaka antare vimukta śastra saṃnyāsam āsthitāḥ dīna mānasāḥ kim hataiḥ asuraiḥ kāryam śastra aśastri kramaiḥ alam jaya siddha phalam kim vā prāṇi hiṃsā ca pāpa dā amarāṇām kṛte kaḥ ayam kim asmākam bhaviṣyati vṛthā kalakalam kṛtvā na phalam yuddha karmaṇā kā svāminī mahā rājñī kā vā asau daṇḍanāyikā kā vā sā mantriṇī śyāmā bhṛtya tvam naḥ atha kīdṛśam iha sarvābhiḥ asmābhiḥ bhṛtya bhūta abhirekikā vanitā svāminī kṛtye kim phalam mokṣyate param yuddham śāmyatu ca asmākam deha śastra kṣati pradam yuddhe ca maraṇam bhāvi vṛthā syuḥ jīvitāni naḥ utsāhena phalam nā asti nidrā evā ekā sukha āvahā ālasya sadṛśam na asti citta viśrānti dāyakam etādṛśīḥ ca naḥ jñātvā sā rājñī kim kariṣyati tasyāḥ rājñī tvam api naḥ samavāyena kalpitam evam ca upekṣitā asmābhiḥ sā vinaṣṭa balā bhavet naṣṭa sattvā ca sā rājñī kān naḥ śikṣām kariṣyati evam eva raṇa āraṃbham vimucya vidhuta āyudhāḥ śaktayaḥ nidrayā dvāre ghūrṇamānāḥ iva abhavan sarvatra māndyam kāryeṣu mahat ālasyam āgatam śithilam ca abhavat sarvam śaktīnām kaṭakam mahat jaya vighnam mahā yantram iti kṛtvā sa dānavaḥ nismṛtya nagarāt bhūyastriṃśat akṣauhiṇī vṛtaḥ ājagāma punar daityaḥ viśukraḥ kaṭakam dviṣām aśrūyanta tatas tasya raṇa niḥsāṇa nisvanāḥ tathā api tāḥ nirudyogāḥ śaktayaḥ kaṭake abhavan a spṛṣṭe mantriṇī daṇḍa nāthe cintām avā patuḥ kasya vā atha vikāreṇa sainikāḥ nirgata udyamāḥ nirasta āyudha saṃraṃbhāḥ nidrā tandrā vighūrṇitāḥ na mānayanti vākyāni rārcayanti maheśvarīm audāsīnyam vitanvanti śaktayaḥ nispṛhāḥ imāḥ iti te mantriṇī daṇḍanāthe cintā parāyaṇe cakra syandanam ārūḍhe mahā rājñīm samūcatuḥ mantriṇī uvāca na śṛṇvanti mahā rājñi tava ājñām viśva pālitām kā daṇḍinī mantriṇī kā mahā rājñī iti kā punar yuddham ca kīdṛśam iti kṣepam bhūri vitanvate atra yat prāptarūpam tat mahā rājñi prapadyatām iti uktvā saha daṇḍinyā mantriṇī praṇatim vyadhāt tatas sā lalitā devī kāmeśvara mukham prati datta dṛṣṭa ḍiḥ samahasat ati rakta rada āvaliḥ tasyāḥ smita prabhā puñje kuñjara ākṛtimān mukhe kaṭa kroḍa galat dānaḥ kaścid eva vyajṛṃbhata bījapūra gadām ikṣu cāpam śūlam sudarśanam abja pāśa utpala vrīhimañjarī varadām kuśān tundilaḥ candra cūḍālaḥ mandra bṛṃhita nisvanaḥ siddhi lakṣmī samāśliṣṭaḥ praṇanāma maheśvarīm tayā kṛta āśīḥ sa mahān gaṇanāthaḥ gajānanaḥ kṣaṇāt cūrmīkaroti sma jaya vighna mahā śilām tatra sthitābhiḥ duṣṭābhiḥ devatābhiḥ saha eva saḥ parāga śeṣa tām nītvā tat yantram prakṣipat divi tatas kilakilā rāvam kṛtvā ālasya vivarjitāḥ udyatāḥ samaram kartum śaktayaḥ śastra pāṇayaḥ sa deti vadanaḥ kaṇṭha kalita akuṇṭha nisvanaḥ jaya yantram hi tat sṛṣṭam tathā rātrau vyanāśayat imam vṛttāntam ākarṇya bhaṇḍaḥ sa kṣobham āyayau sasarjaya bahūn ātma rūpān dantāvala ānanān cañcarīka kulaiḥ agre gīyamāna mahā udayāḥ sphurat dāḍima kiñjalka vikṣepa kara rociṣaḥ sadā ratna ākara aneka helayā pātum udyatāḥ āmoda pramukhāḥ
